Request the Deposed King's Slap in the Face

Causing harm to the country by using intimidation

▲National News Agency, Marseille, 13th: When the deposed King Alfonso of Spain disembarked here today, he was beaten by a Spanish worker. After a doctor's examination, he only suffered a minor skin injury on his right cheek. When Alfonso walked down the suspension bridge, his son Juan was on the ship to greet him and followed him. The worker suddenly stepped forward and punched him. The deposed king was also good at self-defense. His son quickly stepped forward and hugged the attacker until the police arrived and handed him over to the police. The worker, surnamed Messanier, 38 years old, confessed at the police station that he did not intend to seriously injure Alfonso, but only wanted to scare him. He did this because Alfonso caused great harm to the country. As for the deposed King Alfonso, although he encountered an accident, he remained calm and immediately entered a car and drove to the hotel. It is reported that he will go to Paris the day after tomorrow.

World Gold Reserves Estimate

▲Reuters, Geneva, 13th: The final report of the League of Nations Gold Committee, scheduled to be released in June, is said to be unable to agree on whether it is appropriate to maintain the gold standard. The members all believe that the rise and fall of gold is too violent, but they disagree on whether the world's cash will be sufficient thereafter. According to the committee's final report, the world's cash at the end of 1921 totaled 11,349,000,000 yuan, of which 5,864,000,000 yuan were stored in Europe, including 2,683,000,000 yuan in France and 590,000,000 yuan in the United Kingdom. 70,000,000 yuan were stored in Africa, 4,195,000,000 yuan were stored in North America, including 4,051,000,000 yuan in the United States, 353,000,000 yuan were stored in South America, 450,000,000 yuan in Asia, 51,000,000 yuan in Australia, and 28,000,000 yuan in New Zealand.

Observations on Recent Political Situation in Japan

Rivalry between Tokonami and Suzuki factions, Fascist movement becomes apparent

▲Japan News Agency, Tokyo, 14th: Railway Minister Tokonami's plan to purchase private railways is planned to be submitted to the special session of the Diet for approval. At this time of political tension, Okamoto, a member of the Diet from Tochigi Prefecture, suddenly announced his opposition to the plan yesterday afternoon and sent an opinion letter to the Prime Minister and all members of both houses of the Diet. His challenging attitude towards Railway Minister Tokonami is said to be backed by Mori Kanenaga of the Suzuki faction. It is generally expected that this is a conspiracy by Suzuki. Thus, Suzuki's resistance to Tokonami has become apparent. This time, Railway Minister Tokonami is determined to purchase private railways and persuaded Finance Minister to use 30 million yen in public bonds as funding. If this plan can be passed by both houses of the Diet, Tokonami's methods will be recognized by the people, and his success will not only overwhelm the opposition party, but also increase Tokonami's power in various places. The Suzuki faction observed the progress of this situation in advance and openly began to challenge recently, implementing counter-propaganda and hindering the passage of the plan through both houses. The fascist movement problem centered on the military and the vice-chairman of the Privy Council, and the Suzuki-Tokonami opposition problem that occurred this time have already become apparent. The atmosphere at the special session of the Diet is indeed gloomy, and the central political situation is becoming increasingly tense. Important news

Report on Alliance Among England, America and France

Consistent Policy Toward Japan on Northeast Problem

Unwilling to recognize Manchuria as independent nation

Japanese pay the most attention to diplomacy toward France

Correspondent Eito Okuma of Osaka Mainichi Shimbun telegraphed from Geneva that even though the Shanghai issue has ended, the focus of most people is still on the Manchurian issue. When Secretary of State Stimson, who was sailing back to America from Cannes on the 4th of this month, seemed to be focusing on the arms reduction issue on the surface, his major mission was actually diplomatic dealings with Japan regarding the Manchurian issue, discussing a political agreement with the highest officials of the English and French governments. It seemed that in the past, because Secretary Stimson alone led the American actions against Japan, which caused relationships between the two countries to worsen, that this was not a good plan. Therefore he then went on to take unified action with the Allies. Hence after Manchuria became independent, the recognition of Manchuria from each country has become a major issue. Now that Secretary Stimson is using established policy to invite England and France, planning to establish a common policy for the three countries in dealing with Japan, he worked tirelessly to realize the claim, running around in Geneva. According to recent reliable sources, regarding Manchuria, with Secretary Stimson's maneuvering, a political agreement has been established among America, England and France, but the contents of the agreement are not yet clear. However the fact that both England and France are following America's lead and not recognizing Manchuria as an independent nation, cannot be concealed. Therefore, not only must Japan use extreme consideration in diplomacy toward America, but diplomacy toward England and France will increase in importance in the future. In particular, the prior neglect of French diplomacy should now be given great consideration. The world's diplomacy today, in the sphere of international relations, does not allow for ignoring France's influence. Chairman of American naval affairs proposes

Extreme Naval Expansion

▲ Preparing for a Far East War ▲ Also Intending to Warn Japan ▲ Expressing Sympathy for the Weak ▲ Safeguarding Chinese Territory

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reports that Senator Hale, Chairman of the Naval Affairs Committee of the United States Senate, recently introduced a bill to expand the navy to the maximum extent possible based on the London Treaty. The bill was reviewed at a Senate meeting on the 4th. On that day, Hale explained on the floor the reasons for strongly advocating naval expansion. He stated that although the United States is currently standing outside the war zone, it must prepare a sufficiently superior navy for future defense. As for the proposals to reduce the danger of war and reduce armaments, they are not worth considering. The bill I am proposing is based on the position insisted upon by the U.S. representative at the Geneva International Disarmament Conference. The Washington and London naval treaties state that the United States has no danger of war and no need for armaments. It is difficult to acknowledge this kind of argument. Considering the uneasy situation in the Far East, I am paying close attention. The international treaties we once trusted can no longer achieve direct results. The credibility of various treaties has fallen to the ground, leaving no trace. Therefore, it can be said that we are completely disappointed in safeguarding future wars. Moreover, according to the current situation, although the people are tired of hearing about war, most people are still afraid of the imminent approach of war. At this time, I will warn Japan that the United States' naval defenses in the Pacific agree not to strengthen, with the aim of safeguarding China's territorial integrity and the Open Door Policy. Since the Washington Conference in 1922, the United States has been at the forefront of disarmament. Unexpectedly, today the situation in the Far East is becoming more and more dangerous, and the United States Navy is at a very disadvantage. Therefore, it is necessary to change policy as soon as possible and fully expand to the maximum extent possible.

Reasons for the Tight Situation at Yuguan

▲ Talk by the Director of the Yuguan Public Security Bureau ▲ He Zhuguo Refuses Unreasonable Demands from the Japanese

A Beiping dispatch reports that train No. 102 on the Beining Railway arrived in Beiping from Shanhaiguan yesterday (the 10th) at 10:20 a.m. Mr. Lu, the director of the local Public Security Bureau, came to Beiping. According to him, since the League of Nations investigation team went to the Northeast, the Japanese have repeatedly provoked incidents in Yuguan. Local military and political authorities, fearing trouble, have tried their best to prevent it, and the Japanese conspiracy has not succeeded. It happened that a Chinese bandit leader, Wang Dapeng, nicknamed "Flying Horse Fast Gun Wang Er," kidnapped a civilian woman to be his concubine. The woman, resentful, stabbed Wang Er but failed and fled. Wang Er then searched everywhere for the woman to take revenge. The woman, fearing the bandit's ferocity, hid in the Japanese street. Wang searched and harassed in the Japanese street. Therefore, the Japanese military police regarded Wang as a volunteer army and took the opportunity to arrest our Chinese merchants and civilians, entering people's homes without permission, and demolishing the ceiling of the rooms to search for guns. Other acts such as rummaging through boxes and cabinets were even more unscrupulous, causing deep anxiety among the people. On the 5th of this month, several people, including the Japanese Civil Administration Police Chief Okitsuka and Takeda, led 200 Koreans from Jinzhou and others and suddenly occupied the station buildings and the telegraph office. At the same time, a false national flag was erected at the station, with the words "General Headquarters of the Manchurian Empire Border Surveillance Police Team stationed in Shanhaiguan." These false police officers, in groups of three or five, harassed merchants and civilians and interfered with railway administration. After negotiations by local railway staff and military police, no results were achieved. At this time, a Japanese division was increased in Suizhong County, and eight Japanese destroyers came from Qinhuangdao. Other important passes, such as Jiukou, were equipped with gun emplacements and electric nets. After nightfall, the Japanese deliberately fired guns and cannons to disrupt public order, causing extreme panic among the merchants and civilians. Therefore, a Japanese staff officer, Maeda, was sent to the 19th Brigade Headquarters to meet with Brigade Commander He Zhuguo, requesting that he sign a document allowing the Japanese army to have the right to freely dispatch troops to suppress bandits within eighty li of Yuguan. He replied that the bandits in Chinese territory would naturally be suppressed by the Chinese army, and there was no need for others to do it for them. My brigade

Feng Yuxiang's Thoughts

▲ Regretting Jiang Guangnai's Resignation ▲ No News of Chen Jitang Inviting Him to Guangdong

Mr. Feng Yuxiang, who has been recuperating in Mount Tai for a long time, has declined to meet guests, so most visitors have not been able to see him. Recently, a member of Feng's staff gave a detailed account of Feng's recent situation, saying that Mr. Feng's condition has improved, but his phlegm, asthma, and cough have not improved. However, the doctor advised him not to take any more eye medicine, as it would hurt his intestines. However, the recuperation method can not only cure phlegm and cough, but also restore physical and mental strength. Therefore, in addition to writing and reading, he walks in the nearby mountains, forests, and fields, and takes deep breaths in the morning. Because it is suitable for recuperation in a quiet environment, many guests from various places cannot be received in person, and I think everyone will forgive him. As for Mr. Feng's arrival here, it was to avoid trouble and recuperate. He does not often talk about political issues on weekdays. However, his views have been published in various newspapers many times before, and he still remains true to his original intention. As for his feelings, he talked about the news a few days ago that Jiang Guangnai's resignation was about to be approved, and he was very emotional and indignant. Jiang Guangnai was one of the main generals in the Shanghai Battle, and he had contributed to the country and the nation, so he regretted it very much for him. Today, he saw in the newspaper that Jiang Guangnai's resignation had been rejected. The will of the majority of people is always useful. There is no news here of Chen Jitang inviting Mr. Feng to Guangdong, which is probably a misunderstanding. A few days ago, the newspaper reported that Sun Lianzhong had gone to Shanghai on Feng's orders. Just as I was surprised, I saw Sun Lianzhong's denial in the telegram, which has been published in various newspapers, which shows that rumors are unavoidable. Wang Jingwei

(11th) Wan Bi suggests

Last Resort for Disaster Relief

▲ Hold a National Disaster Relief General Donation Week

Our country's disaster relief efforts have been disrupted by the sound of Japanese cannons since the September 18th Incident and the Shanghai Battle. Now the disaster situation in various provinces is becoming more and more serious, and the disaster relief authorities in various places have repeatedly sent urgent telegrams to the Disaster Relief General Association, requesting continued relief. Zhu Qinglan has only raised 7 million yuan in donations from last year to the present and has borrowed 450,000 tons of American wheat, which has long been distributed. Now there is no surplus power to continue to provide relief, and there are still about 60 to 70 million disaster victims in various provinces who have fallen into a desperate situation. I really can't bear to sit idly by. Therefore, I have telegraphed to all parties to appeal and intend to revive the disaster relief atmosphere again and seek the last resort for the disaster victims. Wan Bi, the vice president of the World Red Swastika Society of China and a member of the National Government Relief Committee, specially telegraphed to Zhu yesterday, explaining that since this is the last resort, if the usual methods of raising donations are still used, it may be difficult to obtain good results. Therefore, I suggest holding a "National Disaster Relief General Donation Week," that is, a national general mobilization, for a last large-scale relief. There are still 300 million people in the country, excluding those who are absolutely incapacitated. If each person only donates a few jiao, a huge sum of 120 million yuan can be raised. The methods determined are as follows: First, a national disaster relief general donation will be held. This donation is planned to be held within the shortest possible time from the date of decision, and a national disaster relief general donation week will be set. It is planned to temporarily divide the donation amount into five grades, with the minimum limit being 2 jiao as the starting point, and each increase of 2 jiao will advance one grade, totaling up to 1 yuan. That is, the fifth-grade donation is 2 jiao per person, the fourth-grade donation is 4 jiao per person, the third-grade donation is 6 jiao per person, the second-grade donation is 8 jiao per person, and the first-grade donation is 1 yuan per person. Now, assuming a family of ten, in the lowest limit, the amount donated by this household can be 2 yuan. In the highest grade, the amount donated by this household can be 10 yuan. These five grades of donations will be recognized by the people themselves and will not be forced. However, at least one grade of the lowest grade donation must be recognized. Those who can recognize the higher grades are welcome. Those who can make greater compassionate vows outside of these five grades and independently donate thousands or hundreds of millions of yuan will be especially welcome. Those who donate more money will be recommended by the Disaster Relief General Association to the government for commendation in order to encourage them. Those who can designate special disaster areas, donate huge amounts of relief money, and save the lives of a large number of disaster victims can also be designated by the local government to build statues in the relief area to highlight their good deeds and last forever. In total, the current national population is 450 million people, and the number of disaster victims in various provinces, although there are no accurate statistics yet, is only 60 to 70 million people in total. The majority of people in the country should be able to save this minority of people. Second, we must quickly find ways to continue to borrow American wheat. The 450,000 tons of American wheat borrowed for the flood relief this time, although the distribution in various provinces is not very sufficient and the work relief and agricultural relief cannot be thoroughly relieved, the disaster victims in various provinces have been able to survive from last year to the present, and the American wheat has also been of great help. Therefore, it is advocated that a large-scale final general donation should be carried out quickly to raise relief funds, and the government should still be consulted to quickly continue to borrow a large amount of American wheat and rush to transport it. If the fundraising is slightly successful, the transportation costs can also be paid from it. Suppressing bandits in Hubei Province

Clear Out Within Four Months

▲ Jiangxi and Zhejiang Will Each Transfer a Division to Assist ▲ Funding is Also Being Actively Raised

A Hankou dispatch reports that the Red bandits in Hubei Province have been repeatedly attacked, but they have not been completely eliminated. Last year, there was a Yong disaster, and starving people were everywhere. The bandits used coercion and inducement to replenish their forces. Therefore, the bandit forces became more and more rampant, and it became more and more difficult for government troops to attack. The most heavily red areas are Huang'an in eastern Hubei and Mianyang, Qianjiang, Tianmen, Yingcheng, Jingshan, and Hanchuan counties in central Hubei. Southern and western Hubei are relatively peaceful. Eastern Hubei is the territory of Kuang Jixun's gang, and central Hubei is the territory of He Duan's two gangs. Although Hubei Province is stationed with heavy troops, they cannot be concentrated in one place due to the limitations of the defense zone. However, its recent deployment and funding are more tense than before. According to the investigation of military deployment, such as in the central Hubei area, Zhang Zhenhan, Xiao Zhichu, and Xu Yuanquan's three divisions have all been sent to the front line to prepare for the second general attack. Xu has already taken a boat to Hanchuan on the 12th and transferred to the front to supervise the attack. Western and northern Hubei are paying attention to blocking at the same time. Western Hubei is guarded by the 36th Regiment of the Sichuan Army, stationed in various places and commanded by Wang Lingji. In addition to Liu Maoen's division, northern Hubei also retains a brigade of Fan Shisheng's troops stationed in Xiangyang to assist in blocking the attack. Eastern Hubei is attacked by Ge Yunlong, Zhang Yinxiang, and Peng Zhenshan's divisions, and southern Hubei is attacked by Xie Bin and Guo Rudong's divisions. In addition, there is also a saying that Hao Mengling's division stationed in Jiangxi and Shangguan Yunxiang's division stationed in Zhejiang will be transferred to Hubei to assist in the attack. It is also decided that all districts will be cleared out within four months. As for raising funds, in addition to the 420,000 yuan allocated by the provincial government every month, the Salt Affairs Inspection Office has also agreed to allocate 100,000 yuan every month. However, the Township Clearance Promotion Association is responsible for soliciting public bonds, but it is difficult to raise enough for a while. He Chengjian, the director of the Pacification Office, Xia Douyin, the chairman of the provincial government, and He Hengfu, the standing committee member of the Township Clearance Association, have proposed to mortgage the public bonds for cash to borrow 1.5 million yuan to meet urgent needs. In the future, the gentry and the wealthy will pay the public bonds they should have paid, and a committee will be organized to keep them and be responsible for repayment. As for the formal salary, He Chengjian has forwarded it to the Military Commission and requested an additional 500,000 yuan per month. The Military Commission replied by telegram that it would increase the issuance by 10% from this month. The promissory notes issued were requested by the generals to He and forwarded to the central government for relief. The telegram said, "We have found that the expenses of our troops, since the Ministry of Finance issued 70% of the promissory notes in the middle and late December of last year, the food of the various armies has been in panic. Especially during the Chinese New Year, the difficulties are even greater. We have appealed to the central government to request cash payment. The Shanghai Incident has had an impact, and these promissory notes have become waste paper. The amount of these promissory notes is nearly one million yuan, which is the food that each army should have received after the reduction. During the period before the due date, we still hope to cash them on time. We have borrowed from banks and money houses, and when we cannot cash them on time, we have to find ways to repay the loans from banks and money houses. For several months, the expenses of the various armies have been reduced and discounted, and the unpaid promissory notes have been issued. Even half of the half cannot be collected on time, so that the food of the various armies is always in danger of running out. We cannot make up for the deficit, and we cannot pay back the debt. We have been in a difficult and exhausted state for five months. Now that the bandits are rampant, the supplies of the various armies are so difficult, which has a great impact. We should earnestly request the exchange and issuance to facilitate the bandit suppression. For this reason, we respectfully request that you have compassion for the difficulties and quickly forward a telegram to the central government to urgently seek relief and convert the promissory notes issued to the various armies into cash in installments to be used for repayment and to maintain the status quo. Is this appropriate? Please give instructions to follow. Sincerely, Xu Yuanquan, Qian Dajun, Wan Yaohuang, Fan Shisheng, Xiao Zhichu, Guo Rudong, Zhang Yinxiang, Ge Yunlong, Peng Zhenshan, Zhang Wanxin, Xie Bin, Liu Peixu, Li Zongjian, and Li Dingwu Zhou kowtow." (May 12)

Recent News on the Increase in Business Tax in Zhejiang Province

▲ Officials and Merchants Have Reached a Stalemate

A Hangzhou dispatch reports that the business tax in Zhejiang Province, starting from April, regardless of the standard grade, has been uniformly changed to 10 per mille. Merchants and civilians in various counties have risen up to oppose it, but it has not been resolved. According to Wang Zhuzhai, chairman of the Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce, after the announcement of this case, the association requested exemption from the increase from various Ye Gong associations. The Zhejiang Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce also forwarded the request from the members of various chambers of commerce to withdraw the order. Repeated instructions have been given, all of which are to support the difficulties of the times and persuade various businesses to reluctantly overcome the difficulties. In this move by the government, the tax revenue can be increased by 4 to 5 million yuan per year, which is used to support the finances of Zhejiang Province. However, on the merchant side, the business tax is divided into whole sales and retail sales. Uniformly collecting 10 per mille, some have increased by 4 or 5 times, and some have increased by 8 or 9 times. How much can the merchant power bear? Moreover, it is at a time when the Shanghai War has just stopped, and all industries are reorganizing to seek development. If the increase is one or two times, the retailers may be able to reluctantly overcome the difficulties. Now the increase is too great, and the chamber of commerce advises them to support the difficulties of the times, and the merchants scold the chamber of commerce for not caring about the difficulties of the merchants. Therefore, the two sides are in a stalemate, and it is difficult to resolve.

Wuchang Plane Arrives in Qingdao After Trial Flight

▲ China National Aviation Corporation Expands Tianjin-Shanghai Line

A Qingdao dispatch reports that China National Aviation Corporation is expanding the Tianjin-Shanghai line and passing through Haizhou and Qingdao. It has telegraphed to the Qingdao City Government and the Navy to facilitate it. Today (11th) at noon, the company specially dispatched the Wuchang plane to Qingdao for a trial flight. The city government also sent Secretary Zhang Jianchu to the scene to receive it. Soon, the plane drove to the beach, and a group of people got off the plane, including Zeng Tong, the engineer of the company, Anlison, the chief pilot, Palin, the pilot, and one other Westerner and one Chinese (both assistants), totaling five people. They were invited to the team headquarters by Yang Junjing, the captain of the first squadron of the Navy Air Force, and Wu Guangdou and other team members to rest. It stayed there overnight and flew to Qingdao from Haizhou this morning (11th) at about 10:00 a.m. It plans to stay for one day to survey a suitable location for stopping the plane in Qingdao in preparation for formal air service. It will fly to Tianjin tomorrow (12th). The fuselage of the plane is dark green, with the word "post" marked on both sides. The wings are silver-gray, and the words "China National Aviation Corporation" are written below. It takes about five hours to fly directly from Shanghai to Qingdao. (May 11) Local Communication

▲ Telegraphing to Request the Return of Farmland Used for Airfields

Wuxi

▲ Chamber of Commerce Explains Qian and Silk Industries

Silk factories in Wuxi have suffered losses in recent years and are on the verge of bankruptcy. They are unable to repay the debts owed to the silver and money industries. As the new cocoons are about to be put on the market, all the factories have decided to postpone the repayment of debts, request a reduction in interest, and borrow new money to help them. The Money Industry Guild is the intermediary for deposits and loans. If the loans cannot be repaid, the deposits will also be terminated at the same time. Qianzhuang has no way to turn stones into gold, and it will inevitably not be able to circulate. The decisions made by the silk factories have a great impact on the financial market. A general meeting was convened, and Jiang Huanqing, Chen Songxun, and Cai Yourong were appointed to consult the Chamber of Commerce for their opinions. The Chamber of Commerce believes that the factories borrow money based on their credit. If there are difficulties, they can only discuss solutions based on their past credit. There is no way to make a decision based solely on one-sided opinions. Therefore, it invited various members of the silk factory industry to explain separately and sent letters to the money and silk industries for reference.

Yangzhou

▲ Criminals in the Qishutan Robbery Case Executed by Firing Squad

Qishutan Town, a subordinate town of the county, was robbed by bandits a few days ago, and the police team's guns were confiscated. Later, the police team found guns and stolen goods in Wangjiahe, and the bandits involved in the case, Zhou Shengju (ie Zhou Er), Sun Wu, Shan Huaixi, and Xu Zhaosheng, were arrested in Zhenjiang and sent to the Superintendent's Office for interrogation. The criminals confessed without hesitation and confessed to the cases of robbing Jiangtai Class and the river port Ban Xiaolun. They were sentenced to death in accordance with the Regulations on Punishing Bandits and were taken to the execution ground outside the Fuyunmen bus station on the morning of the 12th for execution by firing squad.

Rugao

▲ Bandits in Yaojiadai Extort Huge Sums of Money

In Yaojiadai, Qin Hu Township, Lugang District, Rugao, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to Zhu Hengtai's house late at night with flashlights and pistols. They broke into the wall and captured Zhu, extorting 400 yuan in cash. Zhu said that there was no surplus money at home. The bandits shouted, "Have you not heard of the Xu Shanfu family in Wangjiadai nearby?" (Xu was robbed and burned once last month and his mother was killed.) If you don't give us the money, we will burn and kill you in the same way. Fearing, Zhu handed over more than 200 yuan in cash. The bandits then took the stolen goods and roared away.

Ningbo

▲ Water and Land Police Team Defeats Gang of Bandits

Hua'ao Mountain in Hua'ao Township, Nantian County, is an isolated island in the sea and is a den of pirates. A few days ago, bandit leader Xu Bangde led more than a hundred bandits to gather on the mountain, and the situation was very rampant. The Water Police Bureau sent the Yongping warship and the Second Water Warship to attack. Magistrate Li of the county also ordered Guo Yao, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to lead more than 40 police and security group members to attack. The bandits stubbornly resisted, and after three days of stalemate, they were broken by the government troops. Four bandits, including Xin Donghan and Zhou Changfa, were captured alive, and six hostages were rescued. The remaining bandits took advantage of the dark night to escape by boat.

Hangzhou

▲ Tragic Incident Arising from a Love Triangle with an Elderly Woman

Qiu Caichun, a farmer from Dongshanwu, Shangsi Township, Hang County, had been living with a 40-year-old woman, Ms. Li, for many years after they became acquainted. Unexpectedly, Ms. Li recently developed a relationship with a stonemason named Shunli, and viewed Qiu as a thorn in her side, leading to frequent quarrels. Yesterday afternoon, Shunli, carrying a wooden club, came looking for trouble and suddenly struck Qiu's head dozens of times. Qiu's head was immediately smashed open, and he died on the spot. Realizing the severity of his actions, Shunli fled the scene. The incident was reported to the police, who apprehended the adulterous woman, Ms. Li, and reported to the Hangzhou District Court for an autopsy. It was confirmed that the cause of death was head injuries. The body was placed in a coffin and prepared for burial. Currently, Ms. Li has been transferred to the court, and a strict search is underway for the murderer to bring him to justice.

Bengbu

▲ Rampant Activities of Communist Bandits in Northern Anhui

The Communist bandits in western Anhui have been rampant for a long time. Although government troops have launched repeated suppression campaigns in the past, the Communist forces scatter and regroup constantly, making it difficult for the government troops to effectively suppress them. Currently, Chen Diaoyuan, the general commander of the First Route Army, is stationed in Hefei and has directed troops to defeat bandit groups west of Liu'an and near Sujiabu. However, Zhengyang in northern Anhui is now facing an emergency. Bandits from Huoqiu, Shou County, Fuyang, and the Henan border have taken the opportunity to join forces and are advancing eastward along the Huai River, threatening Zhengyang. It is reported that Communist propaganda slogans were recently discovered in Zhengyang. Although local authorities have implemented strict defenses, the severe spring famine has led many disaster victims to join the bandit ranks as guides. Yesterday, the bandits approached Zhengyang, causing widespread panic and a tense atmosphere in the town. Today (the 12th), telegraph communications between Zheng and Bengbu were suddenly cut off, and news has been completely blocked. This has caused anxiety and uncertainty in the area. It is currently unknown whether the town has fallen. If it is unfortunately lost, the entire Changhuai area will face serious threats. This intrusion by the Communist bandits appears to be a planned and organized operation. It is reported that the military authorities in charge of suppressing the bandits have telegraphed the central government requesting the dispatch of a larger force for joint suppression.

Important News

Ministry of Education Resident Foreign Consuls

Carefully Review the Registration Forms for Overseas Chinese Schools

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to all resident foreign consuls, stating: "It has been found that various consulates abroad often fail to carefully review the registration forms of overseas Chinese schools that are to be forwarded. On the first day of this month, the Ministry issued instruction No. 110, ordering all consulates to thoroughly review the forms before forwarding them to the Ministry for record-keeping. However, a recent review of the registration forms sent by various consulates reveals that some have been carefully reviewed and found correct, while others still contain errors and have not been properly reviewed, which is a serious oversight. Therefore, the previous order is reiterated. Hereafter, all consulates shall be responsible for carefully reviewing the registration forms of overseas Chinese schools. Any discrepancies shall be returned directly to the original board of directors for correction. After verification and confirmation, the forms shall be resubmitted to the Ministry. The consulates shall be responsible for investigating or supplementing documents as instructed by the Ministry and shall not simply forward them without due diligence." In addition to issuing separate orders, the consulates are hereby urged to comply. This order comes from the Zhejiang Provincial Literacy Promotion Association.

Zhejiang Launches Major Literacy Campaign Today

(Hangzhou Correspondence) The Zhejiang Provincial Literacy Promotion Association has determined that the Third Zhejiang Provincial Literacy Movement Promotion Week will be held in various counties and cities for one week within the period from May 15th to June 14th. Overhaul of Education in Yangzhou

▲ Five Supervisors Jointly Handle Affairs in Yangzhou

｜Teachers Arrested for Claiming Back Pay｜ The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education believes that Yangzhou's education funding has been insufficient for some time, leading to frequent disputes. Director Zhou has specially dispatched five supervisors, including Jin Chongru, to Yangzhou to resolve all issues. The supervisors have been in Yangzhou for over ten days. The following is a summary of the reforms that have already been implemented: (A) Regarding educational institutions: (1) Wang Cai, the principal of Beiliuxiang Elementary School, is mediocre and lacks leadership. (2) Zhu Guangzhao, the principal of Beipailou Elementary School, has inappropriate behavior and tarnishes the reputation of teachers. (3) Guo Yinhuai, the principal of Beimen Elementary School, is a figurehead who neglects his duties and wastes public funds. (4) Jiang Dewei, the principal of Bianyimen Elementary School, lacks effective teaching methods and misleads children. (5) Chen Guantong, the director of the Public Education Center, has been absent from his duties for a long time and has unclear accounts. (6) Wu Hongtu, the director of the Public Library, has unclear accounts and neglects his work. All of them should be dismissed and replaced by personnel selected and appointed by the Education Bureau. This applies to the urban area. Inspections of rural areas have now begun. The results have not yet been announced. (B) Regarding finances: (1) The treasurer is ordered to immediately pay 5,000 yuan to alleviate the urgent needs of educational staff (because Jiangdu education has not paid salaries for eight months). (2) Outstanding education taxes and miscellaneous levies are being recovered. (3) It is stipulated that the Finance Bureau shall collect education funds on behalf of the Education Bureau, and accounts shall be settled daily and reconciled every five days. (4) The treasurer and the accumulation and malpractices of school rental and miscellaneous donations over the years will be investigated. (5) The handover of previous bureau directors will be re-supervised. (C) Regarding administration: (1) The heads of the First, Second, and Third Sections will be changed to clerks. (2) The number of clerks shall not exceed two.

Shanghai Education After the January 28th Incident (IV)

▲ Over 2,300 Unemployed Teachers, Works Confiscated ▲ Oriental Library Lost 2.27 Million ▲ Bookstores Lost 14.067 Million

4. Teacher Unemployment

Education is for life, therefore education is sacred. However, in the past, generals and lords who wore armor and yellow jackets often regarded education as a trivial matter, and were willing to spend the money for cultivating the nation's students on rouge and powder. The income of elementary school teachers was less than that of petty officials' servants, and the income of middle school teachers was less than that of ordinary chauffeurs. But teachers had to maintain appearances, and wear long gowns. They had to be tolerant of the imperial court, ingratiate themselves with superiors, associate with politicians, and dare not offend the gentry. As a result, they ended up demanding salaries due to unpaid wages. But no matter how loudly you cried out and how much you saw it as a matter of national survival, it was ultimately ineffective. After the establishment of the revolutionary government, education was valued more. However, news of teachers suffering from hunger and cold is still frequently reported in the newspapers. Although the salaries of teachers in Shanghai are better than those in the interior, the cost of living is high. Living beyond one's means is common, and there are even those who have not received their wages for the current month even though it is already half over. Schools have suffered greatly from this disaster, and few teachers have escaped being on the brink of starvation. The following are the number of teachers at various levels of schools and the number of unemployed teachers. According to the Municipal Education Bureau, there were originally 2,332 teachers in 33 public and private higher education institutions, 2,793 teachers in 125 public and private secondary schools, and 4,866 teachers in 774 public and private primary schools. It is currently known that 2,396 teachers at all levels of schools are unemployed, including 541 from higher education institutions, accounting for 22% of the original teachers; 663 from secondary schools, accounting for 24% of the original teachers; and 1,182 from primary schools, accounting for 27% of the original teachers. From this number of unemployed teachers, it can be inferred the situation of those now sitting on the cold bench. As for the loss of luggage, books, writings, beloved objects, souvenirs, etc. of the disaster-stricken teachers, the reporter has no way to inquire. I can only briefly talk about one or two examples to conclude this chapter. The following is an example: Mr. Zhou Jifan, who taught at the Patriotic Girls' Middle School, recalled a small story from the disaster. He studied Chinese classics and usually liked epigraphy and calligraphy. On the night of January 28th, he went through many difficulties to escape danger. Among the belongings left at the school were inkpads more precious than opium, stone seals that Bao Yu seemed to value, and a Chinese philology work that he had been working on for ten years. This was the effort of years, and it could not be bought back at any price. Now it has all become a dream at night. Zhou Yueran, an English writer, had all the English literature books he had collected over the years stolen. Liu Shimu of the Nanyang Cultural Research Department of Jinan University lost all his precious collections for studying Nanyang culture. Zhang Feng, an archaeologist, lost archaeological materials, ancient bricks, ancient tiles, ancient tripods, fossils, oracle bones, etc. that he had found over the decades. Yi Peiji's antiques, rubbings, and secret editions were all lost. Everyone has something they cherish in their life. These things may be easily found everywhere, but to find them, one may have to wear out iron shoes and travel all over China, expending a lifetime of effort. After the ruthless and evil artillery fire, I don't know how many thousands of people are sobbing and wailing, holding on to their resentment and anger for the rest of their lives. Unemployment may be short-lived, or there may be hope for re-employment. However, the loss of priceless lifelong treasures will cause permanent trauma to the soul. There is nothing that can comfort this deep wound. At the same time, it is a double blow to the future of culture. The armistice agreement has been signed, but has anyone considered the immeasurable losses of the masses and what kind of negotiations are being prepared to comfort the people?

5. Cultural Tomb

In the past, when people mentioned the Oriental Library, everyone would joyfully give a thumbs up and say, "(This is the only knowledge treasure house in the East)." Now, when people mention the Oriental Library, everyone's face reflects the tragedy in their hearts. The nation's most comprehensive public library, with the largest collection of rare books, has been buried in the gun smoke of the "Siege of Shanghai." It has gone with the spring breeze of 1921. (Heaven and earth may have an end, but this hatred will last forever.) Chinese people, remember it, remember it deeply. How much material value is there in this cultural tomb? Please look at the following list: A. Buildings: 96,000 yuan. B. Books: 2,152,000 yuan. 1. General Books (an average of three or four volumes bound together): 260,000 volumes of Chinese books, 154,000 yuan; 80,000 volumes of foreign books, 640,000 yuan; 5,000 sets of charts and photographs, 50,000 yuan. 2. Rare Books: Classics section, 274 kinds, 2,364 volumes, 1,000,000 yuan; History section, 996 kinds, 10,201 volumes, 1,000,000 yuan; Philosophy section, 876 kinds, 8,438 volumes, 1,000,000 yuan; Literary collection section, 1,057 kinds, 8,710 volumes, 1,000,000 yuan; He Family rare books purchased about 40 million volumes, 1,000,000 yuan; Local chronicles, 2,641 kinds, 25,682 volumes, 100,000 yuan; Newspapers and magazines, 200,000 yuan. 3. Catalog cards: 400,000 cards, 8,000 yuan. C. Business decorations: 28,210 yuan. Total loss: 2,276,210 yuan.

6. Bookstores Suffer Calamity

Since Shanghai became a trading port, it seems to have become the center of various industries in China. Many people say that Shanghai is also the center of culture. If this is true, then Zhabei, Wusong, and other places can be called the center of the cultural center. Bookstores are originally the source of intellectual food for the entire nation. The headquarters of China's only publishing industry is located in Zhabei, and many bookbinding factories are also concentrated in Zhabei. Now they have all been swallowed by the ruthless artillery fire. Every time we think of this, we can't help but feel grief and confusion about the future of culture. Everyone has shed tears of sympathy for the destruction of the editorial office and factory of the Commercial Press and will always remember it in their hearts and minds. There are also several unnamed heroic bookstores that have suffered disasters, but few people know about it. Take this opportunity to tell the people of the country.

(3) Reduced the salaries of supervisors and educational committee members, etc. Currently, all provincial supervisors, except for Yi Zuolin, who went to Xuzhou to resolve the student unrest at Xuzhou Middle School, have set up offices in the county government. Yesterday (the 10th), four teachers who had been dismissed for a long time, Shen Shiyuan, Hu Yanzhi, Li Shousan, and Wang Sun, clashed with Director Jia Qixing when they went to the Education Bureau to demand back pay. They were taken to the county government, and County Magistrate Yang believed that Hu and others were disrupting education and arrested them all, waiting to transfer them to the court for disposition. All the teachers and staff in the urban area were shocked to hear the news.

Disaster-Stricken Secondary Schools

Will Send Representatives to Petition in Beijing

▲ Requesting the Executive Yuan to Approve the Issuance of Cultural Bonds as Soon as Possible The Shanghai Municipal Committee for the Aftermath of Disaster-Stricken Schools held its second meeting at Nanyang Vocational School yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Representatives from Nanyang Vocational School, Guangdong Junior High School, Anhui Middle School, Xinmin Middle School, Patriotic Girls' School, Shibei Middle School, Fudan Experimental Middle School, and Women's Physical Education School attended. First, Zhang Xinsheng from Shibei Middle School reported that Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Education, said, "(The current financial situation is difficult, and although there are no funds to restore Shanghai's cultural undertakings, we cannot but take responsibility for finding ways to help the disaster-stricken schools to recover. In the future, we can issue cultural bonds, using the British Boxer Indemnity as a fund, and the disaster-stricken schools should actively promote the sale.)" However, although Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Education supports the issuance of such bonds, we should unite all disaster-stricken schools in the city to jointly organize a joint committee for the aftermath of disaster-stricken schools to petition the Nanjing government, requesting the Ministry of Education to propose the matter to the Executive Yuan and requesting the Executive Yuan to approve the proposal as soon as possible. The Shanghai Educational Community National Salvation Federation Requests

The Ministry of Education to Provide Relief to Schools in the Songhu War Zone

The Shanghai Educational Community National Salvation Federation submitted a document to the Ministry of Education requesting relief to schools in the Songhu War Zone, which reads: "Submitting a request for relief to the severely damaged schools of all sizes in the Songhu War Zone. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai Incident, areas along the Songhu Railway, such as Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and Paotai Bay, have become war zones. The violent Japanese, relying on their naval, land, and air power, bombed and destroyed school buildings with artillery fire, and scattered books and records. The cruelty of their destruction of culture is even worse than that of Yingzheng. All colleagues in the educational community are heartbroken and furious. Now that the armistice agreement has been signed, it is especially important to restore all schools of all sizes that have suffered in the war zone, so as to avoid the suffering of young people who are out of school. Zi Yu said, 'If there is no propriety above, there is no learning below, and the rise and fall of bandits and people will not have a day.' It can be seen that the method of saving the country is not effective unless we first restore education. However, the losses suffered by various universities, such as Tongji, Jinan, Labor, China Public School, Soochow Law School, Shanghai Law School, Central Medical College, Business School, Chizhi University, and Fisheries School, are estimated to be more than 6.6 million yuan. The losses of secondary schools, such as Wusong Merchant Marine School, Shibei Middle School, Nanyang Vocational School, Hubbei Junior High School, Daozhong Girls' Middle School, Guangdong Junior High School, Huisheng Midwifery School, Lida Academy, Wusong Middle School, and Minsheng Junior High School, are estimated to be more than 2.36 million yuan. The losses of primary schools are also more than 400,000 yuan. More than 127 schools of all sizes have been plundered, with a total loss of assets of more than 9 million yuan. Most of the staff have been sent to investigate, and all schools have submitted damage reports, photographs, and descriptions of the war damage. The losses of other cultural institutions are not included. Moreover, various universities in the country have been in arrears with various expenses for several months. Now, with the damage caused by the violent Japanese, their economic difficulties are even more unbearable. At present, if we want to restore education, we should ask the Ministry to make a comprehensive plan and decide on all practical relief measures, so that schools may have a day of revival. According to the national expenditure statistics, education expenditure accounts for only a few percent. No matter which item is cut, it is not impossible to provide sufficient subsidies. In short, if the Ministry can have good methods and raise a large sum of money to be the nectar of restoring education, it would be a great blessing for the students. If it is not possible, we can only ask the Ministry to issue education bonds, and allocate a part of the British Boxer Indemnity as collateral, so that the fund for culture can be used for the cause of restoring culture. There is nothing better than this. The Ministry bears the responsibility for national education and loves the youth of the country as fathers and brothers love their children. We should share weal and woe and be closely related. This committee is pained by the unending national crisis and awed by the urgency of education. We dare to express our views, hoping to wipe out the shame. All the reasons for requesting relief for the losses of major and minor schools in the Songhu War Zone are included in the document for review and approval. It is for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Education of the National Government. Hu Shuhua, Zheng Tonghe, and Wang Xiaoying of the Shanghai Educational Community National Salvation Federation."

The Municipal Education Bureau Orders All Schools to

Receive Cholera Preventive Vaccine Injections

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to all schools yesterday, stating: "The Department of Health's Official Letter No. 4380 states that everyone knows the harm of cholera. The preventive measures taken by this Bureau over the years have been quite effective. However, this year, the Shanghai area has been in a state of war for a long time. If preventive measures are not taken in time, a major epidemic will inevitably occur. Now that summer has arrived, the Bureau's prevention plan has been prepared and is scheduled to begin administering cholera preventive vaccine injections on the 16th of this month. All teachers, staff, and students of all major and minor schools in this city must complete the injections before the summer vacation. The injection dates will be determined by the Bureau and directly notified to each school. Fearing that the schools may not understand the principle or even resist accepting it, we are hereby writing to instruct all schools to accept the injections to prevent and protect their health. With the approval of this, we have checked that epidemic prevention is very important after the war. Teachers and students of all schools should accept the injections to prevent and protect themselves. The above order shall be complied with."

Record of the Lecture Meeting Held by the Middle School Association

The Middle School Association of this city has been organizing academic lectures, dinner parties, sightseeing tours, and various competitions for teachers and students, such as student speeches, essay contests, and mathematics competitions, every semester for nearly four years, with remarkable results. On the afternoon of the 11th of this month, the association held a lecture meeting at the YMCA of the Eight Immortals Bridge, inviting Dr. Luo Ge and Tao Zhixing to give lectures. More than 120 teachers and staff from various schools attended. First, Chairman Zheng Xigu delivered an opening speech and introduced the two lecturers, Luo and Tao. Then, Dr. Luo Ge lectured on "Education and National Rejuvenation," translated by Zhang Yousan. First, he described the relationship between education and national revitalization in various countries, then analyzed the problems of our country's society, and finally elaborated on how our country's education should solve the problems of society in the future in great detail. Later, Tao Zhixing lectured on "Education of Life," elaborating on the meaning of education as life, giving many examples, and concluding with the unity of teaching, learning, and doing. Afterwards, a dinner party was held, and Ni Wenya reported on the association's affairs.

Improvement of McLellan High School

Since Dr. Xia Jinlin, the principal of McLellan High School on Zhaofeng Road, resigned last year and went to England to serve as the Secretary-General of the Chinese Embassy, Shen Tilan, the former executive of the National Youth Association, was invited to serve as the acting principal. It is now learned that after arriving in London last November, Mr. Xia was invited by Minister Shi Zhaoji to assist the Chinese delegation to the League of Nations in Geneva in handling all important matters. He is still stationed in Geneva. Since Mr. Shen took over the school's affairs, he has been working hard to improve the curriculum, focusing on natural sciences and physical education, adopting the credit system, adding various elective courses, and hiring Guo Dawen, a Bachelor of Science from Soochow University and the former director of the Hangzhou Dawen Plantation, as a biology and natural science teacher, Yan Jiashu, a graduate of the Yenching University Graduate School and a former teacher at Suzhou Taowu Middle School, as a chemistry and mathematics teacher, and Ru Meijun, a graduate of the China Academy of Art and the former editor-in-chief of the World Book Company, as an art teacher. In addition, work has been done on purchasing instruments and compiling forms. It is reported that this session, at the request of the old students, will allow students to re-register within this week, but since the semester is already more than halfway over, they can only study half the course, and they will be given half the credits, and the tuition and food fees will also be reduced by half.

Publication of Kindergarten Administration and Organization

The book "Kindergarten Administration and Organization" is compiled by Ms. Cheng Zhangzhu based on years of experience, in accordance with the latest educational laws and regulations, adapting to the trend of the times, and with reference to the organization of famous kindergartens at home and abroad. The content is divided into four parts, a thick volume in total, with both theory and practice considered. It includes more than 60 illustrations and tables, proofread by Mr. Xu Zhengji of the Municipal Wusong Middle School, and with a postscript by Ms. Xu Wancheng, a professor of children's literature at Shanghai Women's Middle School's kindergarten teacher training program, and a preface by Mr. Shen Baiying, the principal of Shanggong Primary School. It is an essential book for those who study early childhood education and work in kindergartens. The actual price is 50 cents per copy. It is sold at the Shanghai Beixin Bookstore and the Shanghai Women's Middle School Library in Ximen, Shanghai. It has already been published. Sports.

Billiards Masters Performance

｜Amateur Association's Final Act of the Season｜ ▲Medina Defeats Bernal ▲1000 to 777 The Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association invited new and old billiards champions, Medina and Bernal, to perform their skills at the association last night as the final act of the season. Regulations for the Open Chinese Doubles Championship

The Shanghai Chinese Tennis Association announced the regulations for the Open Chinese Doubles Championship as follows: (1) All amateur players in Shanghai are eligible to participate in the competition. (2) The competition is scheduled to start on June 4th. Registration will begin on May 20th and close on May 31st. (3) Those who wish to participate in the competition should register with the Father Laborie Road Sports Advancement Association and pay a registration fee of $3 per team. (4) The competition will adopt a knockout system, with the committee drawing the order. (5) It is stipulated that Slazenger and Siazenger balls shall be the official balls for this competition. If both parties agree, other types of balls may also be used. (6) Except for the finals and the final semi-finals, which will be provided by the association, each week's match balls shall be prepared by the players themselves. (7) All matches will be held on the association's grass courts. (8) Each match will be decided by the best of five sets. (9) Players must hold matches according to the scheduled dates and shall not postpone them without reason. In case of rain or unexpected events that prevent them from playing, the match may be postponed, but the association's secretary must be notified, and the match must be made up as soon as possible. (10) After each match is completed, the winner shall be responsible for notifying the association's secretary of the result on the same night. (11) The dates of each week's matches and the results will be published in local newspapers. (12) The championship team will receive two silver cups donated by Mr. Hu Wulai.

Local News

Note on the Withdrawal of Japanese Troops

The Japanese 9th Division has received orders to depart and return to the country. Commander Ueda has issued instructions. The front-line infantry has successively arrived in Wusong for assembly, preparing to withdraw the first batch starting tomorrow. The Japanese Ministry of the Army has dispatched transport ships such as the Third Daiyuwan to Shanghai yesterday to transport the troops to Hiroshima, Japan, for landing and transfer back to Kanazawa. A Japanese Navy 24th Squadron torpedo boat and a 16th destroyer, carrying a part of Japanese military equipment and ammunition, left Shanghai yesterday to return to the country. Shanghai.

Reopening of the Northern Telegraph Office Tomorrow

The Northern Telegraph Office of the Ministry of Communications, located at the intersection of Laobazi Road and Fusheng Road in Jiande Lane, Shanghai North, suspended its business after the outbreak of the Shanghai War because it was close to the front line. All employees of the bureau temporarily worked in the General Bureau on Sichuan Road. Now that the order in Shanghai North is gradually restored, and businesses in the area have also gradually resumed operations, the bureau, in order to facilitate communication for the nearby merchants and residents, has decided to reopen the bureau tomorrow (the 16th) and resume sending and receiving telegrams from all over the world as usual. In the future, if nearby agencies and businesses need to send telegrams, they can submit them to the bureau for sending, so as to facilitate them.

Overseas Chinese in Southern Indochina Save the Country by Reducing Food

▲Two Million Taels of Silver Have Been Remitted Before and After ▲Funding for the 19th Route Army's Military Expenses During the recent invasion of Shanghai by violent Japan, the 19th Route Army rose up to resist. Since January 28th, it has been more than three months. During these three months, people from all over the country, driven by the same hatred for the enemy, have spontaneously and enthusiastically provided spiritual or material support to the 19th Route Army. The efforts have been great, and especially the donations from overseas Chinese have been continuously remitted to support the army's expenses, with the largest amount. Some have even initiated groups to reduce food consumption and remit the savings to support the 19th Route Army's anti-Japanese military expenses. According to news from Southern Indochina, Vietnam, after the 19th Route Army rose up to resist the violent Japanese on January 28th, giving the Japanese invaders a heavy blow, and the news of repeated victories reached Southern Indochina, the local overseas Chinese were overjoyed. They believed that the 19th Route Army could vent their anger after decades of being invaded and oppressed by the Japanese, and gave the Japanese a head-on blow. Their joy was more than 300 times. Therefore, the overseas Chinese in Southern Indochina at that time enthusiastically donated funds to support the 19th Route Army, and initiated the organization of the Overseas Chinese Food Reduction Association of Southern Indochina, Vietnam, to save military disasters and charities, in order to make it permanent. The association's purpose is to save money by reducing food consumption, support the front-line military expenses during the period of resisting the enemy in the motherland, and provide relief to military disaster refugees. After the war is over, the funds will be used to support national defense construction and shall not be used for other purposes under false pretenses. As for the food reduction method, shops are used as units, and each shop saves 20% of the daily vegetable expenses (for example, if a shop buys vegetables for one yuan a day, it saves two cents), stores it by itself, and pays the saved money once a week. The amount of money received by the association is completely public, and the amount of money received is announced once a week. The association is divided into executive, supervisory, publicity, registration, remittance, and consultation remittance departments. All office staff are volunteers and receive no salary. The initiators are He Dacong, Hu Zhigang, Zhang Yuting, Li Yihuan, Liang Puqing, Wu Jiongzhao, Huang Luzhong, Li Rilun, He Shangping, Cai Jingtang, Huang Yueting, Deng Xueru, Ye Tiansun, Lin Shuru, Yang Zhongfen, Tao Huting, Xie Zhibin, Wen Rongkai, Mai Gansheng, Zeng Gongwei, Zheng Junwei, Liang Zhiye, Zeng Ziming, Mei Fangting, etc. Among them, Lin Shuru and Zeng Ziming are from Minhou, Fujian, and the rest are all from Guangdong. Those responsible for handling affairs are He Dacong, Hu Zhigang, He Shangping, and Huang Luzhong. Those responsible for remittance are Ye Boxing. Those responsible for consultation remittance are Li Yihuan and Huang Yueting. The Nanchang Rong, Kangli, Gongxinglong, Lianyi, Rongxing, Guangfali, Guangnanxing, Meiqun, Meilijian, Taihu, Tianxing, Dongcheng, Xianghesheng, Quanxing, Xiangyuan, Nanya, Anlong, Cuifang, Zhengqitang, Yonghengchang, Yongshenglong, Xieli, Guangdong, Guangyinghe, Junhezhan, Yuanfengsheng, Rongfa, Shenlong, Zhang Jingji, Quanhe, Yongji, Yongmao, Youlan, Shunchang, Hexi, Heshun, Fangquan, Gongchang, Quanhe, Huaxing, Taifeng, Shunan, Fengxing, Taoxinglong, Guanghezhen, Yuanfacheng, Jinxing, Ruizhang, Baihetang, Xingfa, Guangruixiang, Liansheng, Xinya, Boston, Dongdi, Wancaotang, Guangnanan, Jiying, Rensheng, Sentai, Xingshengtang, Juhai, Pingange, Guangshenglong, Tongtai, Shengshengtang, Dongzhan, Tongdongzhan, Qunxing, Shengshengtang, Chengji, Xianyaoju, Jiyuan, Shanghai Company, Tongyu, Wanfutang, Deshengzhan, Tonghe, Ruizhang, Wanyucheng, Wanhuichun, Qiqing, Yongyixiang, Lichangrong, Nianfeng, Gongcheng, Lihe, Xiaohai, Hongfa, Dayou, Liangqiuji, Wuzhuangji, Deli, Liang Tongan, Rongdesheng, Dongyuan, Gengsheng, Lihua, Rongyuan, Guangsheng, etc., more than 100 merchants are directors, and Guangzhao School is also one of the volunteer directors. Tenant Association Holds General Meeting Yesterday

▲Important Resolutions on Tap Water and Rent Exemption The Shanghai Real Estate Association held its 17th membership meeting at its office at No. 98 Beijing Road at 3 pm yesterday to discuss the installation of water meters and the reduction and exemption of rent. More than 30 members, including Chengyu Company, attended the meeting. The resolutions of the various proposals are listed below: (1) Publicly elected Yi Yanfang to succeed as a member of the Municipal Council's Rent Estimation Committee. (2) Tap water case: (A) Notify all landlords to immediately dig artesian wells. (B) Notify all landlords to refuse to sign new contracts. (C) Send a letter to the water company to maintain the original agreement: (A) Water fees are not collected on behalf. (B) One water meter per house. (C) No responsibility for water meter installation fees and deposit fees. (D) Water prices are too expensive. Supplement the original agreement: When the water meter is not fully installed, the water usage is based on the package system and shall not be changed. However, if the water company is willing to directly collect water fees from users, the water fee for package water rent will be deducted truthfully. (3) Send a letter to the Municipal Council, asking why the new contract was not announced in advance to solicit residents' opinions before it was signed and took effect. It is said that the water company even used water cut-off measures, which is disrespectful to the landlords' position and deliberately hinders people's livelihood. (4) Resolved that the method of reducing and exempting rent north of Suzhou Creek shall be handled in accordance with the Municipal Council's method of exempting donations, and requested that the water company exempt water fees during the rent-free period, the electricity company exempt lamp fees, and the Municipal Council exempt land donations.

Regulations Regarding National Product Certificates, etc.

Because the Ministry of Industries recognizes that the regulations regarding national product certificates, etc., were all drafted three years ago by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and that three years have passed, and facts have changed, the clauses have been appropriately revised, and the provincial and municipal governments have been notified to follow them uniformly. The Shanghai Municipal Government has ordered the Municipal Social Bureau to comply. Here is an excerpt of the original order:

Order to implement: Approved by the Ministry of Industries, Document No. 4048. It is about circulating matters. It has been found that the Regulations for Issuing National Product Certificates, Provisional Standards for Chinese National Products, and the Rules of the National Product Examination Committee were all drafted by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce in the 17th year of the Republic of China and submitted to the National Government for promulgation and implementation by ministerial order. Now, more than three years have passed, and there have been considerable changes in the facts. In order to suit the actual situation, facilitate procedures, and adopt the requests of merchants and people, this Ministry has appropriately revised some of the clauses, and has reported to the Executive Yuan and received instruction No. 198 from the National Government for record. In addition to the revised Regulations for Issuing National Product Certificates, revised Provisional Standards for Chinese National Products, and the revised Rules of the National Product Examination Committee, which were promulgated on April 9th by Public Document No. 614 and published in the Industrial Gazette, corresponding copies of the revised regulations and standards are sent to your Municipal Government for examination, and your subordinates are instructed to announce them to the public for universal knowledge. This is approved. A copy of the revised regulations and standards is enclosed, and the Bureau is ordered to comply immediately. This order.

Chinese Goods Entering Germany and Czechoslovakia Not Subject to Additional Taxes

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "To the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, regarding the proposed increase in import tariffs by Germany, Austria, and Czechoslovakia, according to a report from the Embassy in Germany, Chinese goods and Chinese eggs imported into Germany are not subject to additional taxes. This Ministry has already notified you by telegram on April 11th. Furthermore, the Embassy continues to report that, according to the Czech Embassy in Germany, Chinese goods have not been subject to additional taxes since 1927. This is specially telegraphed for your information, and please inform the Egg Industry Association. Ministry of Foreign Affairs."

Lu Zuofu Advocates Going to the Inland

▲ Lecture at the Industrial and Commercial Management Association. The Chinese Industrial and Commercial Management Association held its 29th luncheon meeting yesterday at noon at the United China Association, inviting Mr. He Dekui to speak on the topic of "Industry and Commerce and Domestic Peace." It was learned that Mr. Lu Zuofu, a great industrialist from Sichuan Province, had come to Shanghai, and the association specially invited him to participate temporarily. Although the sky was gloomy and threatening rain, several dozen people attended. Mr. Hu Shuhua, a director of the association, presided over the meeting. After the meal, the chairman briefly introduced Mr. Lu Zuofu, who spoke, saying that the center of Chinese industry and commerce is not in Shanghai, but in the inland, especially in the border areas. Shanghai is merely a gathering place for Chinese and foreign goods. The raw materials for factories here mostly depend on foreign countries, while the resources of the inland are undeveloped, attracting the covetousness of foreigners. Once an incident occurs, there is no way to deal with it. We should advocate the slogan "Go to the Inland." He hoped that the people of the country would learn from the past and strive to catch up, seeking the development of inland industries, so that the Shanghai market could also prosper. Although there are wars and bandits in the inland, if we can bravely go there, it is not impossible to eliminate them. The situation in Sichuan Province is like this, he said. Then, Mr. He Dekui gave a speech, saying that in the past twenty years, our country has suffered from continuous civil wars. The direct responsibility lies with the warlords, but the people cannot unite and strive to stop them. We should also blame ourselves. At a time when foreign enemies are deepening, we should stop internal strife and promote domestic peace. The industrial and commercial circles have a stronger force and are concentrated in cities, making it easier to unite. We hope that everyone will follow the principles of self-help and national salvation, unite and eliminate civil war, and promote domestic peace, so that the future of industry and commerce can also be developed day by day.

Verdict in the "Dangerous Words Daily" Case

▲ The two defendants were each fined. Fan Shuheng from Hubei recently founded the "Dangerous Words Daily" in the French Concession and distributed it in the city. He did not register with the Public Works Department beforehand, and the newspaper did not publish the address of the office. Furthermore, the words and opinions exceeded the scope, which was discovered by Ma Muya (transliteration), the head of the political department of the French Concession police. He believed that it violated the regulations of the concession and hindered public security. It was found that the newspaper was printed by Junyi Printing House at 573 Edward Road. The owner of the printing house, Chen Linyi, was arrested first, and then Fan Zhiping, an employee of the newspaper, was arrested at 61 Xiafei Lane. One hundred and fifty copies of the newspaper and two sets of lead type were confiscated and taken to the police station, then sent to the Second Special District Court. The police charged them with violating the publication law and Article 187 of the French Consul's order. After Judge Zhang Chaozuo tried the case, the defendants hired lawyers to defend them. The debate was declared closed, and the date for the verdict was set. The defendant Chen Linyi was ordered to pay a bail of 500 yuan, and Fan was ordered to pay a bail of 200 yuan, pending verification. Yesterday was the date of the verdict. The defendants and their lawyers went to the court to wait for instructions. At 3 p.m., Judge Zhang presided over the judgment in the First Criminal Court. Fan Zhiping was fined 60 yuan for publishing a newspaper without applying for registration. Chen Linyi was fined 40 yuan for helping to publish a newspaper without applying for registration. If they were unable to pay the fines, they would be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. Before the judgment was final, the number of days of detention would be offset against the fine at the rate of two yuan per day. One hundred and fifty copies of the "Dangerous Words Daily" and two sets of lead type were confiscated.

Smooth Flow of Shanghai-Fuzhou Telegraph

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications on Sichuan Road has been striving to rectify the Shanghai-Fuzhou telegraph communication since the Xiamen submarine cable was taken over, as it is of great importance. The Shanghai-Fuzhou line has now been converted to direct express operation, and a booster generator has been installed at the Quzhou Bureau in the middle, greatly increasing the speed. It can transmit eighty or ninety characters per minute. Those who wish to send telegrams to Fujian Province are advised to use this route as the most convenient.

Striving for at Least One Quarter of Tax Exemption

The Yangshupu Road, Huade Road, Yinxiang Port, Broadway Road, West Huade Road, Jiaxing Road, North Jiangxi Road, North Xizang Road, Haining Road, Aierjin Road, Jielu Road, Han Bili Road, Suzhou Road, and other business associations of the Hongkou District Branch of the Municipal Federation of Citizens believe that the Public Works Department of the Hongkou District has expressed a reduction or exemption of the patrolman tax, but the methods vary. Considering the severity of the damage to Hongkou District, the tax exemption is too small to be fair. Yesterday, a resolution was passed at a representative meeting to send a letter to the Municipal Federation and the Taxpayer Chinese Association, arguing on the basis of reason. The original letter is recorded as follows: We have received your letter regarding the Public Works Department's method of reducing or exempting the municipal general tax. We have found that since the January 28th Incident, the Public Works Department of the Hongkou District concession has allowed the Japanese army to commit atrocities, causing severe damage to the citizens. Even today, most of the businesses have not yet opened, and the scene is desolate. The commercial market has gone bankrupt, and the painful situation cannot be expressed in words. The merchants and people used to fulfill their tax obligations, but now they have lost their right to protection. Exemption from the general tax is a legitimate relief measure. However, the published methods of exempting taxes by district, such as January and February, are completely inappropriate. These inconsistent methods will only cause market disturbances. This case has been submitted to the representative meeting of the Federation's office. The Hongkou District should be exempt from the tax for at least one quarter as the minimum standard. In addition to notifying the merchants and people of Hongkou District to wait for the negotiation to achieve its purpose, so as to show fairness and alleviate the merchants' difficulties, we hereby submit this case for your review and diligent protest, in order to achieve a satisfactory solution. We hope to receive a reply.

The Continental Daily reports that yesterday (13th), according to the Italian Consulate General in this city, a wireless telephone test was conducted between Shanghai and Rome, and the results were quite good.
