After the ship arrived in Shanghai, Count Ciano, the Italian Consul General, spoke to Mussolini, the Italian Prime Minister, and several relatives and friends in the Italian capital on Thursday night, and the conversation was quite clear. It is said that this wireless telephone can be used by anyone traveling on the ship.

Jianghai Customs Discovers

Addiction Treatment Contains Toxic Substances

▲Leiyu Pharmaceutical Company Accused ▲The Two Defendants Released on Bail Pending Trial Cai Yusheng from Guangdong has been running the Leiyu Pharmaceutical Company on Baoshan Road, Zhabei, specializing in selling Cai's Freedom Addiction Treatment Peace Medicine with the Flying Thunder trademark. It has been sold for four years and has been quite successful. The medicine is divided into four types, with the large size being 42 taels per bottle, selling for ten yuan; the next size is 28 taels, selling for five yuan; the next size is 24 taels, selling for three and a half yuan; and the smallest size is 10 taels per bottle, selling for one yuan and five jiao. Until January of this year, Zhabei was affected by the war, so the company moved to No. 22, Sanhe Lane, Jiangxi Road, and continued to sell. On the 25th of last month, the medicine was suddenly discovered by the Jianghai Customs, which reported that it contained a large amount of morphine and opium toxins, and reported to the Narcotics Department of the General Patrol Room. West Inspector Pan Gensi, Chinese Inspector Song Bingzheng, Detective Zhang Yushaoqing, Ding Gao, and others, acting on a search warrant from the court, went to the Leiyu Company on Jiangxi Road and arrested the shareholder, Cui Daosheng from Guangdong, and the manager, Zheng Ziqian from Guangdong. They also confiscated 83 boxes of the medicine, including 54 boxes of 10-tael bottles, 14 boxes of 24-tael bottles, 14 boxes of 28-tael bottles, and 1 box of 42-tael bottles, as well as a bamboo basket containing 19 10-tael bottles, 7 24-tael bottles, 4 28-tael bottles, and 3 42-tael bottles, and 172 taels of opium ash, one opium pipe, one lamp, and one tray, and took them all to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated that the police were prosecuting the two defendants for manufacturing and selling opium substitutes under Article 6 of the Anti-Opium Law, and Zheng Ziqian was additionally charged with possessing smoking paraphernalia under Article 13 of the Anti-Opium Law. This case was reported to the police by the Jianghai Customs, which said that the Leiyu Company was selling addiction treatment with the Flying Thunder trademark, which contained a lot of morphine. The police sent detectives on the 2nd of this month to purchase a small 10-tael bottle from the company for 1.5 yuan and handed it over to the Public Works Department's Health Department for chemical testing. It was found that the medicine contained 13% morphine and could replace opium. Therefore, the court was requested to issue a search warrant, and the above-mentioned medicines were searched and the two defendants were arrested yesterday. The chemical test report and the four types of medicines were presented to the court. According to the Chinese and Western detectives, the defendant Cui Daosheng claimed that he was an advertiser. The Leiyu Pharmaceutical Company had a total capital of 5,000 yuan, with each share being 100 yuan. He had one share. The company was originally in Zhabei, but moved to Jiangxi Road this year due to the war. He was helping out there, greeting customers when they came. However, the medicine was registered by the owner, Cai Yusheng, with the Nanjing government in 1929. He did not know the manufacturing method of the medicine. Zheng Ziqian claimed that he was the acting manager of the Leiyu Company and that he had only been in charge of selling goods since 1930. He did not know whether the medicine contained morphine or anything else. All the smoking paraphernalia were used by his mother, who had now gone to Guangdong, so she left the smoking paraphernalia behind. The opium ash seized was used to make the medicine, etc. Finally, the defendant's lawyer, E Sen, claimed that the Public Works Department's doctor's chemical test report did not determine the amount of morphine or opium in the medicine. It only said that it was consistent with the ingredients of the medicines sold on the market. The words "indeed" in the translation were a mistake. Therefore, he requested that the court reschedule the re-testing of the medicine. Chief Judge Zhou Hanting reviewed the report and instructed each defendant to pay a deposit of 1,500 yuan in cash or property to be released pending trial. The four medicines, large and small, were handed over to the court's forensic doctor for re-examination. The case was rescheduled for trial.

Refugees Return to Shanghai

Tragedy in Huangpu

▲ Two Boats Collide, Three Missing Lu Boyin from Si'an has been running a jute shop in Shanghai. Since the outbreak of the war in Shanghai, Lu moved his family to his hometown of Si'an to take refuge. Now that the situation is calm and the market is gradually recovering, Lu returned to Shanghai on the 12th. He hired Qiu Daosheng's boat in Si'an, carrying Lu's mother, wife, children, apprentices, a total of eight people, and boxes and luggage. Lu was eager to arrive in Shanghai to do business, so he told Qiu to sail quickly so that he could arrive in Shanghai as soon as possible. The day before yesterday, Qiu's boat sailed to Tagang and stopped overnight. Yesterday morning, before dawn, Lu ordered Qiu's boat to set sail. Qiu's boat sailed to a bay at the south end of Shihetang, South Huangpu. Just then, Yang A'jin's boat from Shanghai Hengjihao, fully loaded with sundries, was speeding to the interior. Qiu's boat was unable to avoid it and was violently hit, retreating more than ten yards. The bow of the boat was knocked off, and the boat sank immediately. Lu's family and others woke up in their sleep and cried for help. The boat had already been flooded with water. Yang's boat stopped and lowered a sampan to rescue them. Lu and five of Lu's children and apprentices were rescued. Lu's mother, wife, and an apprentice were missing. Many of the boxes and luggage were lost with the boat. However, Yang's boat, although the bow was damaged, was not hindered and could still sail. Qiu is now holding Yang for negotiation. Yang refused to take responsibility, saying that Qiu's boat had strayed into the wrong waterway, causing the collision. Lu said that the bodies of his mother and wife had not been recovered, and the lost boxes contained valuable items and important account books from the shop. Lu has now instructed his children and others to take a boat to Shanghai first. Lu is waiting there to recover the bodies of his mother and wife.

Gu A'mao Takes Advantage of Martial Law

To Rape a Young Woman

▲Drawing His Sword to Frighten the Villagers ▲The Rapist Plans to Sell the Woman Zhang Yingdi is 17 years old and very beautiful. Since she was a child, her parents betrothed her to Zhang Wenzao of Daijia Village, Jiading, and she was immediately brought into the family as a child bride. During the recent invasion of Shanghai by the Japanese, Zhang Yingdi and others fled from the war zone and took refuge in a shelter in Xieqiao. The day before yesterday, after lunch, Yingdi had an important matter to attend to at her brother Zhang Shunchang's house in Houjia Lane, Zhabei. However, she did not know the way, so she asked her fellow villagers Wu Zhongshan and Qiu A'gen to accompany her. When they were returning after finishing their business and passing near Gonghe Road, they suddenly met Gu A'mao. Gu knew Zhongshan, so he greeted him. After exchanging pleasantries, he saw that Yingdi was young and beautiful, and a bad idea came to his mind. He falsely claimed that the outside was under special martial law and that the Japanese soldiers were very fierce. It would be difficult for them to return to the Nanshi. He thought it would be better for them to spend the night in a nearby inn to avoid danger. Wu and the others believed him and were led by Gu to the Shuanglong Inn, where two small rooms were opened. Gu only had six copper coins in his pocket, so he asked Wu to take off his shirt and pawn it for some money to pay for the room. In the evening, Yingdi slept alone in one room, and Gu, Wu, and the others slept together in the other room. In the middle of the night, Gu suddenly sneaked into Yingdi's room, climbed onto the bed, and tried to commit indecency. Yingdi woke up from her sleep and was shocked to see this. She cried out for help. Gu immediately put his hand on her throat to prevent her from shouting. At that time, Wu and the others heard the sound and gathered together. Gu suddenly pulled out a sharp blade from his side to stop them from making any noise, and said, "You guys get out of this room immediately, or I will cut off your heads." Wu and Qiu were villagers and were so frightened by the sight of the snow-white steel knife that they were numb. They reluctantly withdrew and returned to their room to sleep. Yingdi saw that there was no way to call for help and had to suffer Gu's forcible rape. After the night was over, Wu and the others still accompanied Yingdi back to the shelter. Unexpectedly, Gu followed them to the vicinity of Dadongmen, intending to take Yingdi to another port. Yingdi refused, and they quarreled on the way. They were discovered by Ma Bulong, a policeman from the Third Precinct of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who took them all to the station. During the preliminary interrogation, Yingdi and the others confessed what had happened and requested a strict investigation. Gu A'mao claimed to be 22 years old and worked as a mason, but was now unemployed. Qiu A'gen had lured Yingdi out of the shelter, and he had asked Gu to rape her in the inn to spoil her reputation and make her unable to return. He could then sell her to another port to fulfill his wishes. Now, these people suddenly accused him of forcibly raping the woman. The truth was that he was wronged, etc. As the case involved rape, he was ordered to prepare a document and send it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Woman Commits Suicide in Hotel

▲Claiming to be Xu Difan, a Medical Practitioner At around 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, a female guest checked into the Lao Huizhong Hotel on Shandong Road, Ma Jiaquan. The bellboy led her to room number 12. She paid five yuan on the spot, claiming to be Xu Difan, 30 years old, and a medical practitioner. After the bellboy brought tea, she ordered him to buy some snacks to fill her stomach. After eating, she closed the door and went to sleep. Around 12 p.m. the next day, she had not yet gotten up. The bellboy knocked on the door several times, but there was no response. He then found a way to pry open the door. He saw her lying stiffly on the bed, her body as cold as ice, and she had already died. He immediately reported to the front desk and reported to the Fourth Road General Patrol Room, who ordered the police to come. They carried the body to the opposite Renji Hospital and transferred it to the coroner's office, waiting for the court to investigate.

Taking Advantage of the War

To Form Another Family

▲The Wife Did Not Return Home ▲The Adulterer Detained in the Police Station Sun Yucai, a native of Gaoyou, No. 65 Yangjiadu Street, Nanshi, was a worker. His wife, Sun Dai, was 29 years old. After the outbreak of the Shanghai War, Sun, fearing danger, ordered his wife to return home. Unexpectedly, after several months, there was no news from home. He was very surprised and immediately sent a letter to his hometown to inquire. The reply was that she had not returned home. Sun became anxious and asked people to look around. He learned that she had become intimate with Zhao Yuanshan, a waiter at the Overseas Chinese Bathhouse on Minguo Road, and had taken advantage of the war to form another family in Sande Lane, Jiu Mu Di. He went there the day before yesterday to arrest them both. However, his wife was snatched away by thugs, so he called the police and had the adulterer detained in the First Precinct of the Second District and transferred to the court for investigation.

Doctor Extorted by Bandits

▲Bandits Claim to be from the Three K Party Dr. Tang, who lives in a bungalow in Qiasheng Lane, College Road, in the city, has been doing well in his practice, which has attracted the attention of bandits. A week ago, he received five or six threatening letters, claiming to be from the Three K Party. They said that the party was short of funds and asked for a loan of 300 yuan. Later, a letter even included a bullet and reduced the amount by half, asking for only 150 yuan. They asked him to wrap the money and place it at the foot of the left wall in the lane at 3 p.m. on the 13th. After receiving the letter, Tang rushed to the nearby security corps to report. He also placed a fake package of money. At the appointed time, the team leader of the corps led several team members in disguise to ambush around the lane. At about 3:30 p.m., three people in short clothes arrived. The first person bent down to search under the left wall and was bravely apprehended by the members of the security corps, who arrested all three of them and transferred them to the Second Sub-precinct of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Under preliminary interrogation by the station chief, they confessed that the person who was searching at the wall was named Huang Xiaogou, and the other two were Huang Afu and Huang Zhiming. They said that Wang Laowu had ordered them to retrieve a letter and that they did not know they were committing a crime. Finally, they confessed that Wang Laowu was living in a certain room at the Qingyun Hotel at the intersection of Dongzilaihuo Street, Edward Road, in the French Concession. The station chief ordered several detectives to go to the French Concession police station and arrest Wang Apin, also known as Lao San. He firmly denied being Lao Wu. He was taken to the police station, and after being interrogated by the police chief, he confessed that there were four other accomplices involved in the conspiracy: Li Xiaosan, Luo Changchun, Li A'bao, and Yao Ziqing. After the interrogation, they were handed over to the original police officers and taken back to the sub-precinct, and a report was sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for punishment.

Silk Shop Owner

Returns Home and Encounters Robbery

▲Silk Clothes Robbed Clean ▲Bandits Deceive Him of Ten Yuan Jiading native Zhu Shilin, 43 years old, has been running a silk shop in Jiacheng. Due to the Japanese invasion, the place was devastated. Zhu stopped his business and fled with his family, taking some luggage and renting a place at No. 119 South Wuxi Road. He heard that [Jiading] was now safe. Therefore, Zhu was very anxious and wanted to return home to take a look. However, because the train was not open, he hired a boat yesterday at around 7:00 am. He carried his family and luggage, and set off to return home. Before travelling for a long time, just near Xiaoshadu, Suzhou River, in a remote area, six or seven bandits suddenly came to the shore, shouting fiercely and ordering them to stop. They jumped aboard and robbed a suitcase full of silk and clothes. The bandits carried the stolen goods ashore and rushed into a shed. Shortly afterwards, two bandits returned to the boat and told Zhu that they needed to pay 30 yuan in order to redeem the suitcase. Zhu only had ten yuan on him, so he agreed to pay all ten yuan. The two bandits took the money, went ashore with the other bandits, and disappeared with the stolen goods. Then Zhu recovered from the shock. He separately reported to the police station and the Sixth District police station.

Commercial News

Finance

Gold Price

Swap Day Mediocre

▲Swap Shorts Finally Post Three to Four Tael

Yesterday, as usual, the Gold Exchange began swapping. However, because the 16th is a Western holiday and the market will be closed, the swap was held two days early. The exchange opened at 8 AM. The short side was posting for the June-July swap, initially at four and a half to three taels. It then went to the listed price of four taels and some cents, then four taels and five or six cents. However, the longs quickly swapped, and the price dropped to within two taels, and finally three to four taels. As reported in yesterday's newspaper, all the long and short firms had practically no trading in June, and as usual, they changed to July. However, the opening price was 718.9 taels, and the noon close was 18 taels, a drop of 1.7 taels from the previous day. This was due to the July listing being transferred.

▲July Slightly Softer on Debut

The July contract debuted yesterday, trending slightly downward. The high was only two or three taels. Different firms had unequal trading and there wasn't much volume. It ultimately stood between 715 taels. Initially, the slight drop in silver prices didn't seem to affect it. However, because of the sudden convocation of the American White House for a silver conference, rumors of discussions arose, causing people to feel down, which affected the gold market. By noon, there seemed to be more buyers, and since the foreign exchange rate was neither clearly rising nor falling, it turned mild again. The market will be closed due to Saturday, and also this week's situation has been exceptionally complex. Initially, due to the swap flood, the longs were squeezed, causing the price to rise to 734.1 taels. Then, news of cooperation between Britain and the United States to alleviate the silver shortage caused a sharp decline, breaking 710 taels, and suddenly falling to 708.3 taels, a total difference of 26 taels or so. Overall, compared to last Saturday (June contract), there was a sharp drop of 10 taels. The changes were unpredictable. The details of yesterday's market are recorded below.

▲Market Extremely Dull

Since opening early at 714.5 taels for the July contract, the big firms were returning a quarter. The silver price was only calculated at one-eighth, and private telegrams did not update, so it opened lower. However, Zhi Feng, Yong Qian Chang, Xiang Yuan Kang, and Xiang, etc., bought in, presumably at 17 taels. Yuan Chun, Hong Kang, Yong Heng, Yu, etc., sold, and it dropped to 13.2 taels. With the foreign exchange rate stabilizing, HSBC first absorbed US$31.5625 for September delivery, and Yuan Heng, Yuan Mao, Yong Shun Li, Bing Xing, etc., bought in, jumping 3 taels. By 9:30 AM it was 16.5 taels. Unexpectedly, British and American exchanges were back to 625, and it immediately dropped to 15 taels. Upon hearing rumors of the silver conference being brought up again, Da Xing, Yong, etc., sold off, and it continued to fall by 3 taels. Around 10 AM it was 12 taels. Afterwards, it slightly rebounded, calculated at 13.89 taels, but there was little trading. Da De Cheng, Wu Pin, Ying Feng Heng, etc., bought in, while small firms, etc., sold out. From 10 AM to 10:45 AM, it fluctuated by a few cents or a tael. Later, because US$5625 for August delivery could be settled, and Ri Chang, Xie Xing, Yong Hong Kang Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, etc., were all selling off, the price depreciated again by 2 taels. At 11:10 AM it was only 11.5 taels. Suddenly, it was heard that HSBC was absorbing US dollars for future delivery at 625, and Yuan Heng, Ri Chang, Wu Pin, and foreign exchange hedgers bought in, instantly rising 3 taels. At 11:30 AM it was 14.8 taels. Because small speculators were selling out, it retreated to 13.2 taels. However, material hedgers and Dalian firms were dragging it in, thereby raising the price by 2 taels. By the noon close it was 15 taels, a drop of about 1.67 taels compared to the previous day, excluding the swap. The largest fluctuation in half a day was 17 taels, the smallest was 11.5 taels, with a range of 5.5 taels. The posted price was changed to 787 taels, a reduction of 72-73 taels to 75 taels, then back to 72 taels. The booked amount for May and June was 18 taels, 15 taels for July, supplementary water was 18 taels, and the red line increased by 8.5 taels.

▲Not Much Trading Among Firms

According to surface trading statistics, Yuan Heng, Da De Cheng, Qian Chang Xiang, Shun Li, Wan Xing, and Yuan Kang Xiang were all buying in. Fu Tai Heng, Ri Chang, and Yu He sold out and then bought in. Yuan Mao Yong, Hong Kang Yong, Yuan Chun, and Yi Feng Yong all sold out. Yuan Tai, Heng Yu, Zhi Feng Yong, etc., seemed to be active, buying and selling. However, hedging firms only bought in a small amount.

Exchange Market Clearly Loose, Secretly Flat

Yesterday, the silver market suddenly fell, reversing the five-day upward trend, while the exchange rate continued to decline slightly. The HSBC listing trend was quite different, showing an inverse proportion. It was raised by one level, which is the rate system for British-American exchange. The British gold was calculated at 25, which is one shilling and eight pence; the US dollar was only 25, calculated at 30.5 yuan; Hong Kong remained at 77 taels; the Indian exchange rate added 1.5 yuan; the French franc added 5 yuan; the German exchange rate added 1 yuan; the Japanese yen added half a shield; the Singapore dollar decreased by 1.75 taels. As for the domestic market, the British and American exchanges were initially flat and then seemed loose, but there was no special change, and the fluctuations were very small. Because the gold market had opened swapping, and the price was slightly lower, it was affected by the renewed discussion of the silver conference. By noon, the close was unchanged from the previous day, truly an image of obvious looseness but secret flatness. There was limited trading among banks. The British gold was particularly low, and the US dollar was no more than 2-300,000 yuan, all sold by the gold firms. As for the set-off strips, because there was no market yesterday afternoon due to Saturday, and next Monday is the Western Pentecost, all banks will be closed for one day as usual.

▲British Exchange Internal Market Only Fluctuated by 0625 in Half a Day

From the early market selling price of one shilling, eight pence and thirteen one-two-fifths to three-seventy-fifths, the buying price was three-seventy-fifths to four-thirty-seven-fifths. Hua Bi absorbed half a penny for July, and the noon close was flat.

▲American Exchange Internal Market Only Had a 125 Difference

Near tight and far loose. This month and August-September are actually half a yuan apart. Silk and Tea

Wenzhou Green Tea Has Opened

▲Higher by 20 Taels Compared to Last Year

Yesterday, in the tea market of this port, Wenzhou "Zhen Mei" and "Zhen Mei" needle-shaped green teas from Lailu Tea Firm were officially opened by Jinlong Trading Company. The price of "Zhen Mei" was opened at 80 taels, higher by 20 taels compared to last year, and the price of needle-shaped was opened at 50 taels, higher by 10 taels compared to last year. As for the local "Zhen Mei", transactions were sparse, and the price recognition by traders was as strict as yesterday. Whether the market can develop depends on the French telegram returning to Shanghai next week, which can also be used as a determination, it is said.

Large Quantities of Qimen Black Tea Arrived in Shanghai

Yesterday, the Jiang'an steamship imported more than 1,800 boxes of Qimen black tea. It is heard that there are still more than 4,000 boxes arriving in Shanghai today. It is expected that tomorrow, there will be a huge amount of 6,000 to 7,000 boxes of Qimen tea on the market, which will be a grand occasion, it is said.

Tea News from Anhui, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi, and Supplementary Notes

▲New Tea from Southern Zhejiang Is Being Harvested Immediately

Since the opening of the tea season in Wuyi County, there have only been two or three days of sunny weather, and the rest have been heavy rain and hail, which is unfavorable for picking and processing. The daily picking is reduced by half compared to sunny days, and the tea leaves are heavily soaked by rain, making them hard and not soft, and the kneading and frying process is very labor-intensive. Fortunately, the weather is still cold, and the tea buds are not growing too fast, so they will not become old leaves.

Due to the invasion of the Gan bandits, the new tea in various villages in southern Zhejiang could not be picked and processed. The red bandits who had gathered and fled to Dexing boundary the day before yesterday (the 5th) were urgently pursued, besieged, and defeated by the Jiangxi Provincial Security Regiment, and the situation has eased. Mountain households are taking advantage of this to open their gardens and rush to pick tea, ensuring the livelihood of poor households.

▲New Tea in She County Is Half Harvested and Processed

New green tea from the most famous Jieyuan, Dafang, and Huangshan areas of She County has been harvested and processed by mountain households one week before the Start of Summer to increase the market price of tender buds. However, due to the cold spring and frequent rains, the shipment is slow. The tea produced by each household is about half of the total production. In recent days, the weather has not warmed up, and heavy rains have poured down, which is not conducive to picking and processing. Mountain households have temporarily stopped picking because the mountain tea is still tender. Tea shops in this county are busy transporting goods to foreign countries and opening scales early because the new tea is about to be launched on the market.

▲New Tea in Xiaoshan Is Slow-Moving in Foreign Trading Companies

Jiangtang, Shiliwang, Mashe, Shanxi Yue, and other places at the junction of Xiaoshan and Shaoxing are all tea-producing areas in Zhejiang Province. This year, due to the severe cold in spring, the tea trees in this county budded later, so there was not much new tea before the Rain. Last week, the weather turned warmer, and the first tea was harvested and processed. However, the harvest was not good. Although the selling price of green tea was opened to 120 yuan, the local tea shops in Zhabei, Shanghai, were destroyed by artillery fire, and fewer people opened shops than in previous years. There are few people who come to Xiaoshan to buy tea, so the tea produced by each household is still mostly hoarded and unsold, and the market situation is very sluggish.

▲Weiping Green Tea Has Opened

Weiping in Zhejiang is also a tea-producing area. The annual production and sales of foreign trading companies are no less than tens of thousands of boxes. Since the start of harvesting at the Start of Summer, it is now coming to an end. According to a letter from the area yesterday, the new goods have been officially opened, and the price per dan is 64 yuan, which is 14 to 15 yuan higher than last year. The production in various places has not increased or decreased compared to last year, it is said.

▲Anren and Yugan Tea Suffers from Banditry and Arrears

Anren and Yugan are also tea-rich areas in Jiangxi Province. The tea leaves produced in Yugan, which borders Anren, are inferior in color and taste to An tea, and the price is also cheaper. Most of the annual production is supplied to shops and trading companies, and foreign trading companies rarely purchase it. An tea leaves are tender and can be supplied to foreign trading companies for the production of fine goods. Wuyuan Southwest and Deyi Tea Company used to purchase here. In recent years, Anren and Yugan counties have suffered repeated bandit disasters, and most of the tea trees have been abandoned. Although the new tea in the two places is now suitable for harvesting and processing, farmers are uneasy about farming, fleeing to avoid disasters, and the number of people picking and processing tea leaves in various villages is less than three-tenths of what it used to be, and most of them are extremely poor mountain households who occasionally pick and dry tea to support their lives, and there is almost no tea market to speak of.

Shandong Factory Silk Firm Despite Lack of Price

▲Silk Merchants Insist on Not Selling at Reduced Prices, Market Atmosphere Is Strained

Yesterday, the silk market of this port still lacked progress. It was found that the losses in Europe and the United States were due to the relatively high cost of raw silk, and the losses were still huge, making it difficult to sell. The interest of American companies in purchasing was also weak. The inventory of Shandong Yellow Factory Silk was scarce, and Shandong silk merchants insisted on not selling at low prices. European companies hoped to reduce prices, and the market atmosphere was strained. Yesterday, only Hangzhou silk merchants purchased 10 packages of Shanghai White Factory Silk from Middle Grade Top Grade 18 to 22 strands at the price of 580 taels. Xin Shichang purchased 5 packages of Jinniao Brand Top Grade White Dry Silk at the price of 650 taels. Kechang purchased 3 packages of Heji Top Grade Over-Basin Yellow Silk at the price of 320 taels. Efforts were made to promote the sale of old silk.

Investigation of Silk Inventory in Shanghai Warehouses

▲Total Silk Inventory, Including Old Cocoons, Reaches More Than 40,000 Bales

New cocoons from the mainland will be launched on the market in a blink of an eye, while the number of old silk and old cocoons that are slow-moving in Shanghai is very large. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry have agreed with the leaders of silk and cocoon merchants and the financial community (because old silk and cocoons have been mortgaged to the financial community) on a plan to promote sales. It is found that the old factory silk accumulated in Shanghai warehouses over the years totals more than 20,000 bales, and 100,000 dan of old dried cocoons, which can be converted into 20,000 bales of factory silk based on a reeling conversion rate of 500 catties. Therefore, the total old silk inventory reaches more than 40,000 bales. Overseas silk sales are increasingly sluggish, and there is currently no possibility of dumping, it is said.

Grain and Rice Markets Tightening

▲Yesterday morning in southern Shanghai, due to unfavorable weather, fewer rice boats from the western routes arrived than on the 20th. The inventory in the port is gradually decreasing, and sales in urban and rural stores are not smooth. In addition, it is the end of the lunar month, and firms on both sides are closing their accounts, so the market situation is in a slump. The opening price of Changzhou and Xixi North Japonica rice is fixed. There is not much early rice, late rice, and Feilaifeng in stock. The appetite for Ningbo rice is turning active, although retail sales are limited, and prices are rising sharply. The price of top-quality Changzhou and Xixi rice was similar to before, and the price of Zhongguan rice rose by one or two jiao. Early rice and late rice were still stable. The sources from the mainland include Wuxi, Liyang, Kunshan, Jiangyin, Suzhou, Tongli, Qingpu, Chonggu, Songjiang, and other fifteen or six markets, with a total of about 5,000 dan of river factory rice.

This street also inquired about prices following the market, and the market immediately appeared tighter. However, because the inventory in recent days is sufficient, the supply continues, and foreign firms still have surplus to dump, it is difficult to expect the market price to rise in steps for a while. Improved Sales of Flour in the North

Yesterday, the flour market situation: foreign market prices were reported to be up by a large jiao, and people's hearts turned slightly better. Factory Cloth Fell More Than Rose

Abundant Inventory in the Western Goods Market

After a period of slight activity in fabric transactions, it became flat again. The reason is that there are few days left until the end of May, and the capital of the traders is exhausted, so they all dare not purchase too much. Yesterday, the appetite from Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, and other places was smoother, and the rest were all watching. Prices fell more than rose. Lightweight cloth rose and then softened. 16-pound and 13-pound coarse cloth have a great tendency to gradually decline, and fine twill is even more in a slump. Although the trend of fine cloth is soft, customer sales are still active, with 100 pieces leaving the market every day, which is due to the sales order. The trend of coarse twill is originally weak, and coupled with the unstable situation in recent years, traders from Shaanxi, Gansu, and other places have never purchased in wholesale, so the output is quite small, and the market has no major fluctuations. Under the internal and external pressure, the sales of Western goods are sluggish, which is the highest in recent years, but the supply is still endless. Therefore, products such as Fuchou, white striped muslin, and Yuanyu Fuchou are all flooded in the market. Among them, it is said that the sales of striped Fuchou alone will take three years to sell out. In addition, Eastern goods are also active in recent days, with goods made of yarn and thread selling for only 2 jiao and 5-6 fen, so the sales channels of the shops in this street have been encroached upon. Bleached cloth is also affected by this, so the unfavorable environment is indeed rare in recent years, it is said.

White Lead Sheet Market Conditions Changed

Number 2 white lead sheet is a necessary item for tea traders, so in the previous months, sales were booming. Recently, however, the market conditions have changed. The new tea has already entered the market, and the tea traders no longer need to purchase it. In addition, the export business has not seen any progress, and the market situation is extremely cold. As a result, the standard has fallen sharply. The current market price is 22 taels and 5 qian per dan, which is a drop of about 2 taels compared to before. However, the bottom goods are full, and it is not easy to sell them for a while, so those who are engaged in this business are extremely terrified. Therefore, the standard in the later market may fall again, it is said.

Coal - Kailuan Coal Sales Turn Better

Recently, the coal market in this port has gradually shown improvement. The market is busy with transactions, and the sales of various Kailuan coals are particularly active. In the past two days, the spot transactions reached more than 5,000 tons, most of which were purchased by factories inside the port. Local traders and shops also purchased a lot. The market price is stable. The price of special fine coal is 10 taels, 0 qian and 2 fen and a half per ton, Number 1 fine coal is 9 taels, Number 2 fine coal is 8 taels and 4 qian, and Kailuan lump coal is 9 taels and 5 qian, it is said.

Free Talk

On the Irish Free State (Part 2)

— Kai Xu

Then, two beautiful, naturally talented young women were selected from the Buddhist party. They were both university graduates and resourceful women. So these two women were disguised as country girls, as relatives of fake farmers, and lived together in the countryside. During their leisure time, they took walks in the fields, so they became close to the prison guards. As time went on, they became more familiar with them and even held hands and went on游玩 together, completely forgetting their duties. The date of Fuller's release from prison was set for the afternoon of February 3, 1919. According to prison regulations, prisoners should enter the prison courtyard on that day and do three hours of exercise. Exercise time was from 4 pm to 7 pm. At about 5 pm, the two young women came near the prison. The prison guards greeted them with joy. So they all laughed and joked, or deliberately flirted and whispered sweet words. These prison guards were so fascinated by the beauty that they each led their loved ones to wander in the fields. Unintentionally, they were already far away from the prison. The remaining number of farmers cut off the barbed wire at this precious moment. They opened the back door of the prison with a fake key, led Mr. Fuller out, and six pre-ambushed cars took Mr. Fuller away quickly. The other five created a false front in the rear to prevent them from getting the Fuller car. This is the romantic story of Mr. Fuller's prison break. Mr. Fuller first went to London from prison and then disguised himself as a coolie and crossed the West to the United States. The following year, the British government divided the 26 counties of Ireland to establish the Irish Free State. In 1921, the Irish Free State Treaty was signed between Britain and Ireland. Mr. Fuller had previously said that once the Free State Treaty was concluded, there would be bloodshed in Ireland. Therefore, in June 1922, the Irish Volunteers launched an army to attack the Free State army. It was like the rise of our Northeast Volunteers to fight against the puppet government army. (But is the army of the Irish Free State like the army of the Manchurian puppet state that is incited by the Japanese to bark at its master?) The battle took place in (Dublin), and half of the famous district was reduced to ashes. In the year after that, riots followed one after another, and deaths were numerous. Assassins looked at each other on the road. The deaths of the leaders of the Free State cannot be counted. Mr. Fuller was deeply hidden in the valley at this time. All orders were issued through dozens of people, and even his subordinates could not know Mr. Fuller's whereabouts. Therefore, the Free State authorities had no way to capture him. By January 1923, the party in the Free State prison had exceeded 10,000 people. Mr. Fuller believed that the chaos was causing suffering to the people, so he summoned his subordinates and taught them to give up the struggle. This is the origin of peace in the past ten years. However, now that Mr. Fuller has come out again, can he be like those in our country who advocate democracy and once they enter the central government, they can be as complacent as a king sitting in the south?

Random Notes on Xuanwu Lake in Early Summer

— Zhen Xiang

Cherries are red and ripe, and orioles are singing sweetly. This is the time when gentlemen and ladies gather on the shores of Xuanwu Lake. In recent years, Xuanwu Lake has been carefully managed by the Beijing Municipal Government, making use of its natural terrain and carefully arranging it. The lakeside road has been widened and is now twice as wide as before. The Five Continents Park is bathed in European-style beauty, with green grass and colorful flowers like ribbons. Backed by mountains and facing the lake, the scenery is particularly pleasant. Therefore, the tourists of Qinhuai and Mochou are now attracted by Xuanwu Lake. It is not only the attraction of cherries.

The market price of cherries is not only different in the morning and evening, but also varies from person to person. Often, those who are well-dressed and accompanied by female companions who want to buy cherries are more expensive than others. Usually, we can get one catty for three jiao of洋元 when they first come on the market, but at the most expensive time, we can't get three catties even for one yuan. At the same time, the change in boat price also seems to change along with the price of cherries. When cherries are sold at the highest price, boatmen also ask for very high prices. On the contrary, when cherries are cheap, boatmen will not hoard them. Normally, a big circle around the lake costs only four jiao for a boat carrying five or six people. When it is expensive, you can't get a small boat even if you spend a lot of money.

People from the north of the city who visit the lake used to go directly from Taicheng, which was quite convenient by walking. Now, due to the current situation, traffic on Taicheng has been cut off, and tourists have to detour, which is very painful. It is said that the authorities will remove the obstacles soon to facilitate tourists, but it is still unknown whether this can become a reality.

A few days ago, General Cai Tingkai came to Beijing and made a special trip to visit the lake. A primary school student saw him from a distance and said, "Isn't that General Cai Tingkai?" The general smiled at him. So tourists who heard that the general had arrived all rushed to see the heroic face of the anti-Japanese general.

Extracting Sugar from Wood

— Jia Xuan

Everyone knows that the sugar we eat now is made from sugarcane or turnips, but we have never heard that sugar can be extracted from wood. But we don't need to be surprised. Haven't we become accustomed to all kinds of things that our ancestors considered impossible hundreds of years ago? Extracting sugar from wood may become a very common thing in the near future because it has now been successful in the laboratory and the cost is low, so this method of making sugar is bound to be commercially viable!

Extracting sugar from wood is achieved by using a chemical reaction, | chemically known as (hydrolysis) |. Because we now know that cellulose in wood, if affected by acid, can combine with water to form sugar and other substances. This method of extracting sugar is also very simple: use a barrel and fill it with extremely fine sawdust, then steam the sawdust for about an hour; at the same time, take a dilute sulfuric acid solution (the concentration is one to two parts per thousand, that is, in one thousand parts of dilute sulfuric acid, only one or two parts are pure sulfuric acid, and the rest are clean water.) Heat it to 80 to 90 degrees Fahrenheit, and then pass the hot solution into the bottom of the sawdust barrel and into the barrel, and then flow out from the top of the barrel. The liquid flowing out in this way contains about 2.5 to 3% sugar. Before this sugary liquid reaches the storage tank, it has to pass through a bone ash-filled barrel so that the hydrolysis reaction in the liquid can be fully utilized.

Using this method of making sugar, 30 to 40% of sugar can be obtained from every 100% of sawdust. In the manufacturing process, the consumption of sulfuric acid accounts for approximately 6% of the amount of sugar obtained.

A Record of Military Life in Twin Buildings (52)

— Owner of Qiuxingfu Studio

Chapter 7: Visiting the powerful often makes generals fall, hidden imprisonment in the prison of love allows jailers to become husbands.

The two orderlies were just about to step forward and ask. Suddenly, another person in the gatehouse, having heard the car horn outside, lifted the curtain and glanced out the window. He rushed out to greet the female visitor with a smile, calling out, "Miss Eight. We received your call earlier. Madam Five is waiting for you. Please come in. Go to Madam Five's room and sit down." The female visitor glanced with her beautiful eyes. Seeing the person greeting her, he was fair and handsome, with a slender figure. He wore a well-tailored new khaki military uniform, with an armed belt fastened. He wore a small automatic pistol in a leather holster, without a wooden box. He wore a pair of yellow long boots with spur wheels on the heels. On his shoulders hung small shoulder boards indicating the rank of captain. He looked just like the most handsome young military officer. At first glance, she almost didn't recognize him. Only after a closer look did she smile and nod, saying, "Hey, Deshun. You've really gotten ahead." The one called Deshun blushed slightly and replied sheepishly, "It's nothing. Isn't this Madam Five's special cultivation of me?" So, with questions and answers, they laughed and chatted as they led the female visitor all the way inside. The two orderlies heard clearly, and faced each other, making funny faces, saying, "So she's looking for Madam Five. No wonder that kid waited so intently at the gate. It's none of our business." Having said that, more guests arrived outside the gate. They directed some of the unfamiliar ones to the registry at the second gate. Some of the regular acquaintances would go to the registry on their own without being directed. Then, the registry would consider the order of arrival and divide them into batches, one or several at a time. An officer with the rank of major, holding the visiting cards, would lead them to the reception hall to see Military Governor Ye. Military Governor Ye had a specific time set aside each day to meet guests. There were always around a hundred people seeking an audience. Each batch would chat for a few minutes. From 4 pm to 6 pm, the time was still not enough. He couldn't possibly meet everyone. Either the time was up, or there was other official business that came up temporarily, or he occasionally felt annoyed and tired. Then he would announce the end and tell them to come back tomorrow. If they still didn't get a turn tomorrow, luckily there was the day after. If it was still the same the day after, they might as well wait for him every day for the rest of their lives. It seemed to depend entirely on luck, and the skill of the registry in distributing the large stack of cards into batches at that moment.

Science

Electroplating

— Li

Electroplating has a wide range of applications in industry. Simple experiments are also interesting and easy to do. Any keys or other small metal parts that need to be protected from rust or made more beautiful can be plated with a layer of other metals. In addition, patterns on seals, plants, or coins can be reproduced and are exactly like the originals. Principle: When a solution of a metal salt (electrolyte) is passed through direct current, it decomposes. The pure metal substance adheres to the negative electrode, and the oxygen and acids that combine with the salt adhere to the positive electrode. A. Plating other metals on metal objects. Equipment: 1. One or several 5-4 volt dry batteries. 2. A porcelain container (ordinary bowls or glass cups can also be used). Electrolyte: Any metal salt solution can be used. Here are a few examples: 1. For copper plating, copper sulfate can be dissolved in an appropriate amount of water. 2. For silver plating, one part silver carbonate, ten parts potassium cyanide, and one hundred parts clear water. 3. For nickel plating, five parts nickel nitrate, five parts sodium bisulfite, and one hundred parts clear water. Arrangement: Pour the electrolyte into a porcelain container, immerse the object to be plated and suspend it in the air, connect it to the negative electrode of the battery, and suspend a metal sheet of the same metal as the electrolyte at the positive electrode (a carbon rod can be used instead of a silver sheet for plating a small amount of silver). After several hours, the electroplating is completed. It can be taken out, washed, and polished. Note: Before electroplating any object, it must first be cleaned of rust and dirt with fine sandpaper, washed in dilute sodium hydroxide, and then wiped with dilute hydrochloric acid, otherwise it may not last long and will easily peel off. B. Reproducing patterns. For example, if you have a badge or an ancient coin and want to reproduce its surface pattern, you can first press wax, clay, or plaster on the object to obtain a negative model. Then, lightly coat it with pencil lead powder with a dry brush to make the surface conductive. Then, electroplate it as described above. After it has a certain thickness, take it out and separate it from the mold. Other things such as cloth, plant leaves, and beetles can also be electroplated, which is very interesting. However, due to space limitations, I will not go into detail. In industry, metals such as aluminum, pure iron, copper in the electrical industry, and other extremely pure metals can all be obtained by electrolysis. Therefore, electrochemistry is worthy of promotion.

Chatting About Everything

Amusing Misunderstandings

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

It is a great inconvenience that the language of a country cannot be unified. For example, in our country, each province has its own language, and each county and town has its own local dialect. Our country's language is so complex that it can be called the crown of the world. Often, people are in the same hall, all people from the same country, but because they don't understand each other's language (such as Cantonese and Zhejiang people, Fujian and Jiangsu people...), they have to ask for a translator, otherwise, there will be jokes. My family recently hired a new nanny, who is from Wuhu, Anhui. She calls a (teapot) a (skewer). One day, it was raining, and she said to my mother that she was going to get the repaired (skewer). So my mother misunderstood for a moment, thinking that because it was raining, she wanted to take a car to get the (teapot), so she said to her, (It's raining, you should hold an umbrella, why waste money taking a car?). After arguing for a long time, she finally understood that she was going to get the (teapot). Thinking about it carefully, it was hard not to laugh. Therefore, I thought of a joke that my third maternal uncle told me the other day. He said, (There is a kind of vegetable in the south called (horse basket head), while in the north it is called (livestock basket brain). Because northerners call (horse) (livestock), call (basket) (basket), call (head) (brain)). One day, the master asked the servant to buy (horse basket head) and said (livestock basket brain). This servant was from the south, and although he didn't understand the meaning of the word, he didn't dare to ask too many questions. So he walked all over Beijing (now called Beiping) and didn't know where to buy this (livestock basket brain). Later, after asking others in many ways, he finally knew that it was (horse basket head). This joke of not understanding the language is also enough to make people laugh. At the same time, I also thought of one day, I saw a Cantonese person wanting to talk to a Zhejiang person in a certain place, but unfortunately, they spoke different languages, but they could both speak English. They had no choice but to use English as a temporary substitute for the national language, so they talked a lot in English. I often see Chinese people meeting and speaking foreign languages as fashionable, which always makes me feel sad. The two brothers mentioned in this article speaking English so much is another matter, because they speak different languages, if they don't speak English, then they can only be like the silent Jin people, otherwise, it is inevitable to make jokes. From this, it can be seen that unifying the national language is really an important thing.

▲ Civil First Instance Judgment: Zhonghui Bank Co., Ltd. v. Wu Qizhou, et al., for Debt (Verdict) The defendant shall be jointly and severally liable to repay the plaintiff's mortgage loan of silver 21,888 taels, 5 mace, and 3 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from May 1 of this year until the date of final execution; plus current account silver 9,362 taels and 0.05 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from December 1, 1931, until the date of final execution; plus current account foreign currency 3,051 yuan, 7 jiao, and 4 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from November 9, 1931, until the date of final execution; plus current account foreign currency 3,051 yuan, 7 jiao, and 4 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from November 9, 1931, until the date of final execution; plus promissory note silver 35,000 taels, plus interest at an annual rate of 6% from November 7, 1931, until the date of final execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Ying Minghe, et al. v. Chen Wenbao, et al., for Share Money (Verdict) The defendant Chen Wenbao shall repay the plaintiff 3,300 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from April 14 of this year until the date of final execution. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The defendant Chen Wenbao shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Zhu Xiangrong v. Xu Yuefan, et al., for Debt (Verdict) The defendant shall be jointly and severally liable to pay the plaintiff silver 9,010 taels, 0 mace, 4 fen, and 4 li, and foreign currency 6,418 yuan, 6 jiao, and 4 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from December 1, 1931, until the date of final execution. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Lu Zhi v. China Xingye Bank, Yin Shisheng, et al., for Deposits (Verdict) The defendant shall be jointly and severally liable to repay the plaintiff 9,720 yuan, plus interest at an annual rate of 8% from April 2 of this year until the date of final execution. This judgment may be executed provisionally if the plaintiff provides a security deposit of 3,000 yuan. ▲ General Liquidation Office of China Mao Ye Bank v. Zheng Quan for Debt (Verdict) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 460 yuan and 3 jiao and 5 fen, plus interest at an annual rate of 1.2% from January 1 of this year until the date of repayment. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Xu Jianting v. Li Zhixiang, et al., for Goods Payment (Verdict) The defendant Li Fukang shall repay the plaintiff 440 yuan, 0 jiao, and 7 fen and 2 li. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The defendant Li Fukang shall bear one-half of the litigation costs, and the plaintiff shall bear one-half.

Weihai Automobile Company for a goods payment dispute, which this court is executing, has already had the debtor's personal property sealed, appraised, and auctioned. As no one purchased the property by the deadline, in accordance with the previous price, the lowest price has been reduced by 10%. The auction date is now set for May 23rd. The court will dispatch a clerk and police officers to conduct the auction at the location of the personal property. All residents who wish to purchase the said personal property shall come to the Clerk's Office of this court for instructions in order to be led to the location for viewing, and then comply with the deadline for purchase. If there are two or more bidders, the person with the highest bid shall be the purchaser, and they shall pay the full price in silver on the spot, and the auctioned property will be given to them for collection. All residents are hereby notified. Special notice is hereby given. (Items to be auctioned) (1) Auctioned Item: One No. 177314455 automobile. ▲Police Department v. Qin Wangshi et al. Opium Case (Main Text): Qin Wangshi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of one hundred yuan for the crime of providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. Wang Achi's sentence is suspended for two years. The opium pipes, "red pills," and other items shall be confiscated according to the list.

Half a pound of opium dross shall be confiscated and burned.

▲Criminal Ruling: One Item: Zhu Yisheng's request for bail for Jiang Xinfu: It is known from the petition that the defendant Jiang Xinfu in this case has been sentenced to one month of imprisonment and should be executed according to law. The request for bail is difficult to approve. This is the ruling.

▲Civil Ruling: One Item: Chen Jiyan's statement that he is being detained overdue and requesting clarification: It is known from the petition that the Second Special District Prison previously sent a letter on February 26 stating that the prisoner's term of imprisonment would expire on the 25th of this month and he should be released before noon on the 26th. The attached civil suit was sent to the court for execution. The prison's execution upon the expiration date is in accordance with the law and there is no possibility of being overdue. Furthermore, the period of detention has not yet expired. After repeated court hearings, he was ordered to provide bail. He should quickly find a guarantor for verification. Furthermore, the creditor Gao Guiting has been requested by letter to Zhejiang Shaoxing Court to assist in summoning him for questioning on the 21st of this month. He should be informed of this ruling.

▲One Item: Qiaji Trading Company, Lu Gaoyong's request to receive funds: It is known from the petition that the requested amount of three hundred yuan should be received at the court at 9:00 AM on the 16th of this month for issuance. As for the remaining debt, the court previously scheduled a hearing for the 7th of this month, but the petitioner did not appear on time. The debtor Xu Hengzhi has continued to pay three hundred yuan, which should also be issued. He should be informed of this ruling.

▲One Item: Lachi Mangxing's request for execution: It is known from the petition that the hearing was previously scheduled for March 5, but the petitioner did not appear on time. The request should be re-filed and executed upon re-notification. However, he should comply with the time limit and appear in court to verify. This is the ruling.

▲One Item: Xu Shouchong's request for continued execution: It is known from the petition that this case has been scheduled for a joint hearing at 2:00 PM on May 23. The petitioner should appear on time. This is the ruling.

▲One Item: Gu'er Baikesin's request for execution: It is known from the petition that the case has been appealed. The request should be postponed for discussion. This is the ruling.

▲One Item: Juyuanhao, Guo Shuopeng's request for prompt execution: It is known from the petition that this court has already sent a letter to the French Concession Public Works Bureau to revoke its demolition permit and issued a notice prohibiting its demolition. He should be informed of this ruling. The original judgment of the First Special District Local Court should be temporarily stored. This is the ruling.

▲One Item: McLean Motor Company Liquidator Wei Quan's request to reject the acceptance of Xinyi Bank v. McLennan case: It is known from the petition that this court does not have a Xinyi Bank v. McLennan case. He should be informed of this ruling.

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch

▲Public Notice Service: One Item: Chen Yikang v. Wang Zhonglian Debt Dispute Appeal Case (Main Text Posted in the Court's Display Area). Main Text: The appeal is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Criminal Judgment: Zhang Xianjun Robbery, Intentional Homicide, etc. Combined Case Appeal (Main Text): The appeal is rejected.

▲One Item: Zhang Guangzhen Endangering the Republic of China (Main Text): Zhang Guangzhen is sentenced to five years of imprisonment for jointly promoting doctrines incompatible with the Three Principles of the People with the aim of endangering the Republic of China. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. The reactionary books, leaflets, and other items shall be confiscated.

▲One Item: Zhang Yunqing et al. Endangering the Republic of China (Main Text): Zhang Yunqing and Zhang Zongshun are each sentenced to five years of imprisonment for jointly promoting doctrines incompatible with the Three Principles of the People with the aim of endangering the Republic of China. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. The reactionary books, leaflets, and other items shall be confiscated.

▲One Item: Sun Zhishan et al. Endangering the Republic of China (Main Text): Sun Zhishan and Mao Zhentai are each sentenced to eight months of imprisonment for jointly preparing to subvert the government by illegal means. Liao Chengyi, a recidivist, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for jointly preparing to subvert the government by illegal means. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. The reactionary books, leaflets, printed materials, and other items shall be confiscated. Wang Afang and Gu Zhiming are found not guilty.

▲One Item: Yang Fuqing Using Counterfeit Currency Appeal (Main Text): The appeal is rejected.

▲One Item: Sun Zhiyao Robbery Appeal (Main Text): The original judgment is revoked. Sun Zhishan is sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for joint robbery. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment.

▲One Item: Chen Axiao Theft Appeal (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. Chen Axiao's sentence is suspended for three years.

▲One Item: Lin Afu Endangering the Republic of China (Main Text): Lin Afu is found not guilty. Thirteen copies of the "Youth Workers' Gazette" shall be confiscated.

▲Civil Judgment: One Item: China National Products United Emporium et al. v. Huizhong Silver Company Debt Dispute Appeal (Main Text): The original judgment is amended, except for the dismissal of the appellee's claim for insurance fees, attorney fees, and litigation costs. The appellants, National Products Emporium and Hong Yanbin, shall repay the appellee a sum of 20,000 taels of silver in eight equal installments, with each installment due every month starting from the 7th of this month, plus interest at a rate of 5% per annum from the date the original promissory note became due until the date of full repayment. If they are unable to repay, the appellants Fang Jiaobo and Zhuang Zhihe shall repay on their behalf. The remaining appeals and incidental appeals are rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Gu Zhicheng v. Su Jiaxin Loan Appeal (Main Text): The appellant is rejected. The third-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Qu Yenuofu v. Di Maisi Compensation Appeal (Main Text): The appeal is rejected, and the third-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Criminal Ruling: One Item: Wang Yuezhen's Protest Against Hua Guochun's Injury and Infringement of Freedom (Main Text): The protest is rejected.

▲One Item: Zheng Qingtang Abduction Request to Suspend Detention (Main Text): The request is rejected.

Shanghai Local Court

▲Criminal Judgment: Zhang Ziqing Theft Case: Zhang Ziqing is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for theft with accomplices. The number of days of detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment.

▲Qu Simao et al. Theft Case (Main Text): Qu Simao and Shen Xiaomao are each sentenced to six months of imprisonment for theft with a group of three or more people. The number of days of detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment.

▲Wu Liegou Robbery Case (Main Text): Wu Liegou is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for each of the three counts of robbery, to be executed for a total of eight months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment.

▲Li Zhenming Opium Case (Main Text): Li Zhenming is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of ninety yuan for transporting opium substitutes. If the fine is not paid after forced execution, one yuan shall be counted as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. Eighty taels of "red pills" shall be confiscated.

▲Chou Chengyu et al. Robbery Case (Main Text): Public prosecution against Zhu Fuxiang is not accepted.

▲Shen Chang'an is found not guilty. Chou Chengyu and Wang Da are each sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for jointly entering and robbing with a group of three or more people. The number of days of detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment.

▲Ruling: Pan Zhu Hou et al. Fraud Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected.

▲Zhang Zhifeng et al. v. Defendant Suspected of Fraud and Intimidation Case (Main Text): This private prosecution is rejected.

▲Gao Shunbiao v. Defendant Suspected of Fraud Case (Main Text): This private prosecution is rejected.

▲Civil Judgment: Gu Wushi v. Zhang Dian'an Debt Appeal Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The litigation costs of this instance and the third instance before the remand shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Zhu Runxing v. Tiancheng Dyehouse Rent Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff a rent of 225 yuan and shall return the leased land of 6.58 hao on Liyuan Road. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Wu Zhanglin v. Wu Heshang Demolition Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Qu Jianzhang v. Huang Juming Guarantee Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff a guarantee of 320 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Chai Bingquan v. Zhang Yigong Loan Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff a loan of 85 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Yan Huihai v. Yan Jishi Tenancy Rights Appeal Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.
